Onke amalungelo agodliwe. 
Akukho ngxenye yaleli bhuku engashicilelwa kabusha, igcinwe noma yenziwe esinye isimo, 
kungaba ngokufothokhopha, ukuqopha noma ngayiphi enye indlela ngaphandle kwemvume 
ebhalwe phansi yabashicileli. Lowo oyokwenza noma yini engagunyaziwe mayelana naleli bhuku 
uyobekwa icala noma ahlawuliswe kanzima. 



AMAZWI OKUBONGA 

Ngibonga ngingaphezi nenhlangano yababhali Usiba 
ngokusingatha lo mncintiswano ngobuchwepheshe obusezingeni 
eliphezulu. Ngibonga nezinjulabuchopho zoSiba ezisethulela 
izifundo zokulolonga ababhali. Okuningi engikuzuze kulezi 
zifundo kube neqhaza elikhulu ekwenzeni lo msebenzi ube 
sezingeni elincomekayo. 

Ngingelokothe ngikhohlwe wukubonga Dkt. Nakanjani G. 
Sibiya ngeqhaza alibambile ngokufaka imibono yakhe ephusile 
ukuze lithi thuthu izinga lalo msebenzi. Ume nje Sotobe! 

iii 



ISAHLUKO SOKUQALA 

Wabe uzoqala ngelesithupha umcimbi. Bobathathu 
babeqale ngokubheka ekhasini elabe linohla lwamagama alabo 
ababezokwethweswa iminyezane. Okunye bakufunda emva 
kokuba sebelibonile igama likaNqoba Mzobe. UThobile 
walibona maqede wahlengezela izinyembezi. Ingqondo yakhe 
yasuke yagijimela esehlakalweni okwabe sekwaphela iminyaka 
engamashumi amabili nambili senzeka. Walikhumbula ibhungu 
elabe limeshela uthuli, kodwa yena engakazimiseli ngokuqoma 
ngoba esafunda ibanga leshumi nambili, elalibizwa ngebanga 
leshumi ngaleso sikhathi, ezitshela ukuthi uyoze aqome esezoqeda 
ukufundela ubudokotela. Walukhumbula ngokucacile usuku 
mhla lelo bhungu limhlukumeza ngokumdlwengula, kanti 
usezokhulelwa lo Nqoba othweswa iziqu ze-LLB namuhla. Uvalo 
lwamshaya kwabanda amathumbu ngesikhathi ekhumbula ukuthi 
wake wasikaza kaningi ukusikhipha leso sisu. Lwalumshaya 
kufanele, ngabe wabulala isibhaha sommeli. 

1 



Kuyiqiniso ukuthi injabulo ike iphenduke usizi, kanti 
nosizi luke luphenduke injabulo. UThobile wayesaphuphuma 
injabulo, esanda kuliphasa ngamalengiso ibanga leshumi 
nambili, ebona kahle ukuthi wabe ezokwemukelwa kalula 
oPhikweni lwezokufundela ubudokotela eNyuvesi yaseNatali. 
Konke kwabe kumi ngomumo ngoba no-Lynne wabe esevumile 
ukumkhokhela ngesikhathi efundela ubudokotela. Dedelele, 
bohlololo, esethola ukuthi ukhulelwe, sekufanele ukuthi 
ihlehliswe indaba yokuyofundela ubudokotela. UMaNdelu owabe 
engumsebenzi sasezindlini wabikela umqashi wakhe u-Lynne, 
owathukuthela wathelwa ngamanzi. Wathatha izinyathelo 
zomthetho, waphumelela. Ukuphumelela komthetho kwaba 
ngokwesikhashana ngoba kwathi lapho umfanyana eseneminyaka 
emithathu nengxenye ubudala, kwasolakala ukuthi wabe 
esengozini yokubulawa. UMaNdelu wayisusa ingane kwa-A 
eMlazi yahlala naye e-Westville, emzini ka-Lynne. Abelungu 
ababengomakhelwane basheshe bamceba uLynne ukuthi 
wabe ehlalise ingane yomdabu endaweni yabamhlophe. Wake 
wazama ukusebenzisa inkanyana yakhe yobummeli, kodwa 
wagcina ehlulekile. Imithetho yangaleyo minyaka yabe ivumela 
izisebenzi kuphela ukuba sezindaweni zabelungu. Kwadingeka 
ukuba umfanyana lo ayohlala ezihlotsheni emakhaya. Wathi 
angahlanganisa iminyaka eyisithupha yobudala wamukelwa 
e-Little Flower Primary School eShowe; wafunda ehlala 
ngaphakathi esikoleni. Yisikole esizimele lesi, kanti iningi 
lezingane ezifunda kuso ngamaKhaladi. UNqoba uphasa 
i-LLB nje selokhu afundiswa ngu-Lynne kusukela ekuqaleni. 
Ukuqala komcimbi wokwethweswa kweziqu kwawubuyisa 
umqondo kaThobile kulezi zinkalo owabe usathilileka kuzo. 
Lathi lingezwakala iculo lokwethweswa kweziqu elithi: 
“Gaudeamus igitur, juvenes dum sumus...” yasukuma yonke 
indlu isihlonipha inhlabaluhide yezicukuthwane zezifundiswa. 
Nebala, zangena zihamba ngemigqa emibili, ziyikazela amajazi 

2 



emibala ehlukene, nezigqoko ezime ngokufana zahlukana 
ngemibala. Zathi zingahlala phansi, laphaya phambili, nendlu 
yahlala phansi. UMphathi wawuvula ngesizotha umcimbi, 
kwethulwa izicukuthwane ezithile, kwalandela inkulumo yosuku. 
Yona-ke yelanywa wukwethulwa kweminyezane. Kwaqalwa 
ngababephasele ubudokotela kwezomthetho, kwehla njalo 
kwaze kwafikwa kwababephase i-LLB. Umsindo wokuhalalisa 
wabe ulokhu uba mkhulu njalo nje uma kubizwa abomdabu. 
Abanye babehalalisela ngokukikiza. Kwake kwasukuma nenye 
insizwa endala yagiya iqonde phambili lapho sekubizwa 
igama lomzukulu wayo. Yabe ibona kahle ukuthi yayingeke 
iphinde ilahlwe yicala njengoba kwabe sekukhona ummeli 
emndenini. Lwaqhubeka uhlelo kwaze kwafikwa ezibongweni 
eziqala ngohlamvu ‘m’. Lamenyezwa igama likaNqoba Mzobe, 
“Nikhoba Mazobe!” Kwakungasho lutho ukuthi sabe silibize 
kabi isifundiswa somlungu; okubalulekile kwabe kungukungena 
kwalo emabhukwini amakhulu. Laya phambili izenzana lomfana, 
laguqa, labekwa uphawu lwezifundiswa ezinqobile. Bashaya 
ihlombe bekikiza o-Lynne benoMaNdelu. Bakitazeka abomdabu 
bebona umlungu ekikiza, nokwenza ehalalisela owomdabu. 
Ihlombe likaThobile laphazanyiswa wukwesula izinyembezi ezabe 
zimenywe ngumunyu owamgubuzela ngokuzuma. 

* * * 
Kuyimpicabadala ukuthi isidalwa esingumuntu sibe nonya 
nesihluku esedlula konke okuphansi komthunzi welanga, kodwa 
sibe saphefumulelwa umoya kaNkulunkulu. Lo mcabango 

3 



wafikela uZine MaZikhali Mbili ngesikhathi ephuma esangweni 
lomuzi wabaqashi bakhe abasha eMhlanga Ridge, eThekwini. 
Kwabe kungoLwesine, okuwusuku lwekhefu kubasebenzi 
zasezindlini, luphinde lube wusuku lokudumisa kulabo besifazane 
asebazikhethela iNkosi. Ufikelwa yilo mcabango nje yingoba 
usuke wabona izinsizwa ezimbili zizidlulela ngomgwaqo laphaya, 
wabe esekhumbula amadodana akhe amabili okwabe sekwaphela 
iminyaka adlula emhlabeni ngendlela ehlasimulisa umzimba. 
“Ukuba abafana bami kababulawanga ngabe sebakhula baba 
ngakayana,” kucabanga uMaZikhali eqhubeka nendlela eyabe 
imsondeza ezintweni zokuhamba. 

Imali yamakhambi yayimsiza kakhulu uMaZikhali 
ekufundiseni amadodana akhe kanye nasekulungiseni umuzi. 
Kwabe sekuneminyaka uMbili abhunguka, waziyela kwanhliziyo 
ngiyise. Amahemuhemu ayemkhomba eGamalakhe ngase-Port 
Shepstone, lapho ayehlala khona nesitetelegu sentokazi eyabe 
imhlophe sengathi yiKhaladi. 

Yabe iqale kancane kancane, yathi isuka yabe ibhebhetheka 
indaba yokuthi uMaZikhali wabe ethakatha. Abanemiqondo 

4 



ehluzekile bavele bazibonela nje ukuthi wabe ebhecwa ngobende 
inyama engayidlanga umntanomuntu. Abanye balibeka 
ngembaba elokuthi lezi zinkulumo zabe zisuswa ngumona. Nakhu 
phela wabe uya ngokusimama umuzi kaMaZikhali, nakuba 
ayengesenamyeni. “Lo mfazi uzenza indoda. Phela usesibukisa 
ngezwe uma esewulungisa kanje umuzi wakhe,” kuphawula 
enye indojeyana eyabe isinswanswa njengoba labe selisesinqeni 
nebhodlela likagologo eyayilikhwelele. 

Basuke beqinisile uma bethi umuntu akafi uma ingakakhali 
insimbi yakhe. Kwabe kuseyilo oLwesine, uMaZikhali ecelwe 
ngabelungu bakhe, oMnumzane noNkosikazi Shaw, ukuba 
angalali kwakhe eMawoti, abuye ntambama ukuze abheke 
izingane kusihlwa ngoba babezohambela umcimbi othile. Baze 
babuya phakathi kwamabili. UMaZikhali bamfica ezumeke 
kanye nezingane khona ekamelweni lazo. Kabaphazamisanga. 
Bageza, balala. Kusaphele amahora amabili bezumekile abelungu 
bakaMaZikhali, kwangena ucingo lwasendlini. Lwezwakala 
lukhala kakhulu kunokwejwayelekile, lukuphazamisa kakhulu 
ukuthula kwasebusuku. Wathi gubhu uNkosikazi Shaw, 
walucosha. “Hello,” esho ngezwi elabe lisindwa wubuthongo. 
Lakhuluma ngesiZulu izwi lowesifazane owabe ekhala kalusizi. 

5 



“Can you speak English, please,” kusho uNkosikazi Shaw ethukile. 
Izwi lowesifazane okhalayo lasibhidilisha isiNgisi. “Zine’s house 
fire, fire, fire! Boys died! Everything ashes, ashes, ashes!” Umbiko 
wacaca bha kuNkosikazi Shaw, wangakunaka ukuqhuzuka 
kwesiNgisi. 

Waya esula izinyembezi ekamelweni lezingane. Wathi 
angakhanyisa, amehlo agijimela kuMaZikhali, adlulela 
ezinganeni. Bonke babezumekile, belele kamnandi. Kwaba 
yisikhathi ebabuka, ecabanga, elokhu esula izinyembezi. 
Wakubona kuyingozi ukuya ebusuku endaweni yesehlo. Wagcina 
enqume ukuwethula sekusile umbiko kuMaZikhali. Waphindela 
ekamelweni lokulala, wakhonga ubuthongo. 

“I thought this black-on-black violence was now a thing of the 
past,” kuphawula uMnumzane Shaw ekuseni, encinciza, enikina 
ikhanda. 

“The have-nots will always hate the haves,” kuphendula 
umkakhe echiphiza. Bavumelana ngokuthi uNkosikazi Shaw 
ayise uMaZikhali emaphoyiseni ukuze abaphelezele bayobona 
umonakalo emzini wakhe. Kwake kwaba ngumzukuzuku 
ukuthola ubuciko bokwethula udaba olusinda kanje 
kuMaZikhali. Wayilanda ngokufingqiwe indaba yosizi 
lukaJobe waseBhayibhelini, eyiqhathanisa nobunzima bempilo 
yasemhlabeni kanye nesihluku sesidalwa esingumuntu. 

“Sale usuyibhadlaza indaba. Sebezibulele izingane zami, 
akunjalo?” kubuza uMaZikhali uvalo lubhakuzisa isifuba 

6 



sakhe. Avume ngekhanda uNkosikazi Shaw, yehle impophoma 
yezinyembezi kubo bobabili. Asheshe azikhuze, azibambe 
uNkosikazi Shaw, aduduze uMaZikhali, amnike neduku 
lokwesula izinyembezi. Emva kwemizuzwana uNkosikazi 
Shaw achaze ngocingo lukaQalisile. Wabe engomunye walabo 
ababesizwe nguMaZikhali ekutholeni abantwana. 

Bafika kumagebhugebhu lapho kwakukade kumi khona 
indlu kaMaZikhali. Lawo magebhugebhu ayebiyelwe ngebhande 
lepulastiki ephuzi ebhalwe ngamagama amnyama ukuthi: 
‘Police’. Abantu babemi izixongololo belangazelele ukubona 
okwabe kwenzeka esizeni. Amaphoyisa ayelokhu ebahebeza labo 
ababesondela kakhulu baze bathinte nomngcele wepulastiki. 
Ochwepheshe bezomlilo babematasatasa bezama ukuthola 
imbangela yokuqubuka kwawo. 

Lacishe lasangana ikhanda likaMaZikhali ngesikhathi ebona 
izingebhezi nogalo bamathambo amadodana akhe. “Awu, 
izingane zami! Izingane zami! Awu, ngaze ngasibona isihogo 
ngamehlo enyama!” Lokho kumpongoloza kwabe kuphelezelwa 
yimpophoma yezinyembezi. Kwezwela kwabanye, zehla nakubo. 
Wathulisa, waduduza udadewabo kaMaZikhali. 

“Ungamthulisi. Myeke adazuluke. Akufanele agqibelane 
ngaphakathi,” kweluleka uNkosikazi Shaw ngesiNgisi esilula, 
ekhuluma nangezandla ezama ukucacisa. 

7 



“Awu, naze nangingcwaba ngiphila bantu baseMawoti!” washo 
ephelelwa ngamandla eyetha uMaZikhali. Bamtatamisa bamfaka 
evenini ayelethwe ngayo. Iphoyisa labaphindisela eMtshebheni. 
Imoto kaNkosikazi Shaw yasuka eNanda yaqonda kodokotela 
e-Redhill. UMaZikhali welashelwa ukwethuka nengcindezi. 
UNkosikazi Shaw wababeka KwaMashu, waphuthuma 
emsebenzini. 

Emva kwamasonto amabili, alothiswa ngabangcwabi 
amathambo ezelamani. Umlotha bawuthela olwandle oMaZikhali 
benodadewabo, ebahambise ngemoto uNkosikazi Shaw. 
UMaZikhali akaphindanga walubhada eMawoti. Wagcina 
ungatholakalanga umkhondo wezinswelaboya. Selokhu kwathi 
nhlo umphakathi uyesaba ukusiza abomthetho ngobufakazi 
obungaholela ekuboshweni kwezigebengu. Kakufiki kumuntu 
ukuthi wesaba nje kungase kugetshengwe yena ngokuzayo. 
Ukuhamba kwesikhathi kuyawapholisa amanxeba nezingozi, 
kusale izibazi eziyobe zilokhu ziwulondoloze njalo umlando. 
Kwaba njalo nakuye uMaZikhali. Zazingasoze zashabalala izibazi 
zomphefumulo ezaziqhakambiswa wukuthi wabe esemdala 
engasenakubathola abanye abantwana. 

Abakwa-Shaw baphakamisa ukuba uMaZikhali afake 
isicelo sendlu yomxhaso ngase-Verulam. Yena wanquma ukuba 

8 



kuxhunywe ikamelo emzini kadadewabo KwaMashu, azihlalele 
naye. Abelungu bakhe basemukela isinqumo, bamxhumela 
amakamelo amabili. Kwaba lula lokhu ngoba izingane 
zikadadewabo zabe zisebenza komaGoli nako-Richards Bay, 
esazishonela kudala nomyeni wakhe. 

Emva kweminyaka sadlula isehlakalo saseMawoti, abakwa-
Shaw banquma ukulifulathela leli amabombo bawabhekisa 
e-Ireland, okungesinye seziqhingi zeGreat Britain. Wenqaba 
waphetha ukuhamba nabo uMaZikhali ngesikhathi bemcela. 
Bakhathazeka kakhulu emoyeni njengoba wabe esemdala, 
kungaselula ukuba athole omunye umsebenzi. Umuzi wabo 
kanokusho wathengwa yisiqumama sakwaLanga esabe sisuka 
komazakhele bakwa-D eMlazi. Abakwa-Shaw bake bathi 
ukugoba amadlangala izinyangana ehhotela eThekwini 
ngesikhathi kusalungiswa imicikilisho yokuthengiselana indlu. 
Ngalezo zinyanga abakwaLanga babekhokha i-occupational rent 
yomuzi wabo omusha. UNkosikazi Shaw wacela i-agent eyabe 
ibathengisele umuzi ukuba imxhumanise noNkosikazi Langa. 
Injongo yakhe kwabe kungukucela abakwaLanga ukuba baqashe 
uMaZikhali. Yabahlanganisa i-agent, kwaxoxwa. UNkosikazi 
Langa wavuma ukuqasha uMaZikhali izinyanga eziyisithupha; 
aqhubeke nokusebenza uma egculiseka yindlela asebenza ngayo. 
Uthatha lesi sinqumo nje uNkosikazi Langa yingoba usekhathele 
wukuhlushwa ngamantombazane ayekade esebenzela abelungu, 
anyanyalate lapho esesebenzela abomdabu. Lokhu ayekwenziswa 
yinkolelo embi yokuthi owomdabu akufanele asetshenzelwe kahle 

9 



sengathi ungumlungu. Balifulathela leli sebekhululekile emoyeni 
abakwa-Shaw, bemshiye esesebenza uMaZikhali. 

AbakwaLanga babethole indodana eyodwa. Kwase kuphele 
iminyaka emihlanu yaganwa, kodwa lutho ukuthola abantwana 
umakoti. Phela kuvamisile nje ukuthi abantu abagidlabezwe 
ngengcebo bancishwe inzalo. Bafika eMhlanga Ridge nje 
sebelilahlile ithemba emva kokwehluleka kwemizamo yodokotela, 
izinyanga kanye nabathandazi. Lesi simo wasibuka maqede 
samthinta uMaZikhali wafisa ukubasiza abakwaLanga, nakuba 
ayesanquma ukwehlukana namakhambi ngenxa yesehlakalo 
saseMawoti. Wabona ukuthi ukungabasizi kwakufana 
nokwenqaba ukusebenzisa isiphiwo abe esinikwe nguMdali. 
Nakho nje ukuhlangana kwakhe nabakwaLanga ngale ndlela 
wakuthatha njengesu loMdali. 

Saya ngokuya sikhula isifiso sokusiza abakwaLanga kulesi 
simo, kodwa abuye athiywe wukuthi kwakungenzeka ukuthi 
izicwicwicwi lezi zabe zingakholelwa nhlobo emithini yesintu. 
Kwaphela izinyanga enqikaza, wagcina ezidele amathambo 
waxoxa noNkosikazi Langa. Wachaza nangalabo ayesebasizile, 
nangezigigaba ezabe ziholele ekutheni anqume ukulugodla usizo 
lwakhe. Washo nokuthi naye sabe siwuhlupha umoya wakhe 
isimo ayesibona. 

“Ngiyakuzwa MaZikhali. Sengithandazela ukuthi iNkosi 
yenze umusa, uphumelele umzamo wakho nakulezi zingane. 
Ngiyazi ukuthi izinto lezi zinabantu bazo. Omunye umuntu uke 
asize abantu ngapha nangapha, uye kuyena umagange, kodwa 
kungalungi okwakho,” kuphawula uNkosikazi Langa ecabanga. 

“Kona kuyiqiniso okushoyo. Kodwa-ke bekungakaze kwenzeke 

10 



kimi lokho. Akekho owake wabuyela emuva elambatha. Ngabe 
kuqala ngani. Futhi-ke umoya wami ungitshela ukuthi nani 
nizophumelela Sothole.” 

“Ewu, singathini mntakaNzimase? Kuningi nje bo 
osekwadungeka. IsiZulu sethu sesaba nezibhidi. Sekuyosiza khona 
nje ukuba kulokhu kulungiswa lapha nalaphaya njengoba wenza 
nje,” kuchaza uMaZikhali eze enqekuzisa nekhanda. 

“Ayi, ngibongile bandla. Ngizokhuluma nazo izingane 
ngizwe ukuthi zithini zona. Angithi nje usuyokuzwa ngami,” 
kuphetha uNkosikazi Langa. Wazizwa efikelwa yithemba elisha 
emva kokukhuluma noMaZikhali. Umbuzo owabe uhlupha 
umoya wakhe nsuku zonke wabe uthi: “Liyodliwa ngubani 
leli lifa elingaka uma indodana yethu igcina ngokungabatholi 
abantwana?” Zonke izinjinga ezingenabo abantwana noma 
abazukulu, zihlale zigqilazwa yilo mbuzo. 

“Awu Ma, yiziphi lezi enizidingida isikhathi eside kangaka 
nino-Anti MaZikhali?” kubuza indodana kaMaSishi noLanga. 

“Hawu, kanti usubuyile? Cha, Ntuthuko mntanami, siciciyela 
yona le ndaba yenu ninomakoti. UMaZikhali uthi usesize 
abaningi. Ukukhuluma kwakhe kuyalivusa nakimi ithemba.” 

“Mina Ma ngisola ukuthi izinto zoniwa yilesiya sihluku 
sikababa,” kuphawula uNtuthuko ekhombisa ukukhathazeka 
emoyeni. 

“Habe, wabala isihluku sikayihlo, wayeka esakho?” kubuza 
uMaSishi sakudinwa. Athi angabona kuqhamuka umakoti 
kaNtuthuko ehlise izwi, buthi ukuswabuluka nobuso. “Dlula 
ngapha makoti mntanami. Cha, akusilo udaba olutheni. Le 
ndaba yenu isize yezwela nakuMaZikhali. Naye usafisa ukuzama 

11 



ngamakhambi akhe. Uthi baningi impela ebasiza. Ngithe ngizoke 
ngikhulume nani ngizwe ukuthi nithini.” 

“Kona kunjalo MaCele mntanami. Kodwa-ke singamethemba 
uMaZikhali, uhlakaniphile. Futhi-ke useyinkakha kulesi siphiwo 
sakhe. Yizimfundamakhwela ezivamise ukwenza amaphutha.” 

“Ayi, kulungile ma. Mtshele ukuthi sivumile ukuthi asisize,” 
kuphetha uNtuthuko ngokushesha. Ufuna kusheshe kudlulwe 
kulolu daba nje yingoba unovalo lokuthi unina angase aphahluke 
athinte nokuyimfihlo yomndeni. 

12 



ISAHLUKO SESIBILI 

Kwaba yizinyangana nje uNqoba esebenza no-Lynne 
enkampanini yakhe, wamtholela umfundaze owamyisa e-Harvard 
College, eMelika, esayoqhuba zona belu izifundo zomthetho. 
Yithuba eliyivelakancane leli, yingakho alemukela ngazo zombili, 
waliphathisa okwezikhali zamaNtungwa. U-Lynne wayeposelwa 
imiphumela yaleso naleso sivivinyo, ukuze naye athokozele 
izithelo zemisebenzi yakhe. Nakhona lapha, uNqoba wenza kona 
kanye ayedume ngako, ukuphasa ngamalengiso. Lezi zindaba 
zamthokozisa kakhulu ukhulu wakhe uMaNdelu. Wayemqambe 
leli gama ngoba efuna ukuthi anqobe njalo nje. UNqoba wathi 

13 



angaphothula e-Harvard College, waba nesifiso sokuthi ake athi 
ukusebenza khona eMelika, efunda ngeposi. Kwaba njalo. 

“Ngifuna ube ngumakoti wakwami Philile. Ningafanelana 
kahle kakhulu nendodana yami,” kusho u-Lynne ntambama 
ngelinye ilanga eyobeka uPhilile ezintweni zokuhamba ngoba 
izulu labe linomoya owabe uncinzancinza kabana. Ethuke 
uPhilile, abuyise izinhlonze. 

“It can’t work. My mother would disown me,” kulandula uPhilile 
enikina nekhanda. Ahleke kakhulu u-Lynne. Amangale nje 
uPhilile ukuthi ngabe ukitazwa yini kangaka lo mlungu. U-Lynne 
avule ikhosombana laphaya phambili emotweni, phambi kwakhe 
uPhilile, akhiphe imvulophu enkulu ayinike yena uPhilile. 

“Uyothi ungathola isikhathi uphe iso. The other two ladies are 
his biological mother, who is a medical doctor, and the older lady 
is his grandmother; she works for me at home,” kuchaza u-Lynne 
ngesikhathi enika uPhilile imvulophu eyabe ingavaliwe thaqa. 
Wayemukela imvulophu, wayiphatha eyibhangqe nesikhwama 
sakhe. Sabe sisincane isikhwama sakhe, ingenakungena kuso 
imvulophu. Wacabanga ngokushesha uPhilile, wayithola 
impendulo yombuzo owabe uhlupha ikhanda lakhe. Wafuna 
isiqiniseko salokho ayekucabanga, wasithola. 

“ls he your son by adoption?” kubuza uPhilile ebheke u-Lynne 
owabe ebheke phambili, eshayela ngokucophelela. “Sort of. 
Yes, you could call it that. But not legally.” Imoto yafika erenke 
yamatekisi aya eSiphingo. Wabonga, wehla uPhilile. 

Washeshe wayithola itekisi eyabe iya eSiphingo. Esehleli kuyo, 
wake wasikaza ukuyivula imvulophu ka-Lynne kodwa wabuye 

14 



wazikhuza ebona amehlo emaningi. Wathi angehla eSiphingo 
wabamba eya ekhaya kwaMakhutha. Wafika amehlo emaningi 
nasekhaya ngoba wabe esefikile umfowabo omncane u-Boysie, 
nemanzi ebazalayo. Wabe engazimisele ngokuthi bazibone lezi 
zithombe ngoba lokho kwakungase kuqubule imibuzo eminingi 
abe engenazo izimpendulo zayo. 

Wazibuyisela emvulophini izithombe, wathula ecabanga. Kona 
kungumqondo omuhle ukuhlekisana nomuntu owenza umsebenzi 
ofanayo nowakho. Kuba lula nokusizana kulokhu nalokhuya. 
Lo mfana ubukeka enomqondo ozikile; akabukeki neze 
eyilabatheka. Wacabanga ilabatheka okwabe kusaphele izinyanga 
eziyisithupha ahlukana nalo. Wabe ecasulwe wukuthi wayethole 
ukuthi liyinkunzi yohlobo, likhulelisa ubuthaphuthaphu. 
Bahlukana nje selinezingane eziyisithupha zamantombazane 
ayisithupha. Kusobala ukuthi emva kweminyakana nje lalizokube 
selakhe isizwe sonke. Umuntu owenza kanje usuke engenawo 
nhlobo umqondo ozikile. Umqondo wakhe usuke uzintantela 
emoyeni nje. Usuke engazicabangeli lezo zingane ahamba 
ezizala kuwo wonke amaqele lawa. Zivamise ukuba yizigebengu 
izingane zabafana ezikhula zingahlali noyise. Lokhu kungenye 
yezimbangela zokugcwala kwentsha emajele. Ukuba ngumhlambi 

15 



kazalusile lokhu kuzidonsela ekubeni yimfuyo yasemajele. 
Wathi angafikelwa yilo mcabango uPhilile, ingqondo yakhe 
yagijimela kumfowabo u-Boysie. Wayethe angaphasa ibanga 
leshumi nambili, wasishiya phansi isikole, wathi usekhathele 
wukugqolozelana nezincwadi yena. Unina wathi ayikho into 
angayenza uma umuntu ezigwaza ngowakhe, ecekela phansi 
ikusasa lakhe. U-Boysie wayengeke asiyeke kalula kanje isikole 
ukuba wabe ekhona umuntu wesilisa ekhaya. Walibona nephutha 
likanina lokuthola izingane zize zibe mbili engashadile, nokwenza 
azithole kubantu abehlukene. 

“Wenze kahle kakhulu wayishiya ekhaya. Yigcine kanjalo nje. 
Ngiyokutshela uma sengiyidinga. Okwamanje ngifuna ubajwayele 
bonke abakuleziya zithombe ngoba uzokuba yilunga lomndeni 
wethu.” UPhilile wahleka kancane ngoba wabe ecabanga ukuthi 
wabe ezintelela nje u-Lynne, kodwa wathi lapho embheka wathola 
ukuthi wabe engadlali. Washeshe wabona ukuthi wabe eyile 
nhlobo ephikelelayo uma ifuna into. 

U-Lynne wabe ekuqonda kahle ukuthi umlilo ongakhwezelwa 
uyalotha, kwenyele nokudla okuphekwe kulelo ziko. Yena-ke 
wayengafune kudla okunyelile. Wayikhwezela indaba kaPhilile 
noNqoba. Kwathunyelwana izithombe, kwashayelwana 
izingcingo, kwaphetha ngokuthi uPhilile ake athi hulukuqu 
amasonto amabili eMelika. 

UNqoba no-Lynne balekelelana emalini yokugibelisa uPhilile 
ibhanoyi; yena wathi ukuthasisela kokokugqoka, wathenga 
nezimonyo. Wazibona enenhlanhla engandile, ukuthi athi eqala 
ngqa ukugibela ibhanoyi, avele aye ezweni eliyingqwele yomhlaba 
kwezomnotho, ezobuchwepheshe kanye nokunye okuningi. 
Unina wameluleka ngokuthi akhiphe umthakathi, ukuze abe 
lula, aphile kahle. Zalungiswa izincwadi zokuhambela kwamanye 

16 



amazwe, zalungiswa ezempilo njengokuthola imijovo edingekile 
nokunye. 

“Mhh! Niyofa nizilanda Philile mntanami. Uya eBoston, 
e-United States of America! Kuhle lapha-ke ukulalela uma 
umuntu simeluleka sithi makafunde. Bangaya nje laba ababalekela 
isikole? He, bangaya ungahleka!” kubhuqa unina kaPhilile 
noBoysie. 

“UMa ngeke nje akhulume aze aqede engangicibanga 
ngemicibisholo yamazwi. Ayi, ngisanibonile,” kusho uBoysie 
enyukubala ephuma. 

UPhilile wayethe ukuligwegwisa kancane iqiniso. Wabe 
ethe uvakashela umngane wakhe omdala ababefunda naye 
eyunivesithi. Wayengelokothe atshele umfowabo nonina ukuthi 
wabe evakashela isoka lakhe. Inhlonipho yobuZulu kayikuvumi 
nhlobo lokho. Wayengamhlebela udadewabo ukuba wabe enaye. 
Ukusondela kosuku lokuhamba kwandisa nezeluleko. ULynne 
wamtholela ayezobe elokhu ekuhogela uma ezwa inhliziyo ithi 
canucanu ngesikhathi esebhanoyini. Wamluleka nangokuthi acele 
ukubhukelwa isihlalo esiseceleni kwewindi ukuze abone amazwe 
ayezondiza phezu kwawo. UNqoba wameluleka ngokuthi aze 
aphathe ipheya lezicathulo ezithambile, ezithe ukumxega kancane, 
ezinezithende ezimfuphi. Wamchazela ukuthi ukuhlala isikhathi 
eside ebhanoyini kuvuvukalisa izinyawo, njengoba igazi lihamba 
kahle uma unyakaziswa wonke umzimba. 

UPhilile wayiswa yintombazane engumakhelwane 
esikhumulweni sezindiza, eThekwini. Waphelezelwa ngunina 
noBoysie. ULynne bamfica eselinde khona esikhumulweni 
sezindiza efuna ukuqinisekisa ukuthi ifezeka ngempela imizamo 
yakhe yokwakhela uNqoba ikusasa elihle. 

17 



Indiza kaPhilile yasuka ngehora lesihlanu ntambama iphikelele 
eGoli. Wehla kuyo wangena ngaphakathi esakhiweni sesikhumulo 
saseGoli. Wenyuka ngezitebhisi ezihambayo, sezimyisa lapho 
babeqoqene khona ababezothatha izindiza ezihambela kwamanye 
amazwe. Eyakhe yasuka ngehora lesikhombisa kusihlwa. Kwabe 
kungenye yalezi zinkunzimalanga ezintweza emoyeni kuthuleke, 
kube sengathi zimile kazinyakazi nhlobo. UPhilile wake wathi 
ukubuka ngefasitela. Wabona esala ngokushesha amafu emkhathini, 
kwaba yikhona kumcacela ukuthi inkunzimalanga le igijima 
ngempela. Banikwa ukudla kwakusihlwa kungakahlangani ngisho 
nehora besukile eGoli. Ngehora leshumi izintokazi ezinakekela 
abagibeli, zabanika obhulankethe abancane, abambathisa imilenze 
kusukela emathangeni kuya ezinyaweni. Emva kwalokho, 
kwacishwa izibani kwadlalwa ifilimu. Laphaya phambili kwakudlala 
isithombe kuphela. Ofuna ukuzwa inkulumo nemisindo 
kwakudingeka asebenzise ama-ear phones. Nawo ayenezinkinobho 
ezimbili, eyomculo neyefilimu; umgibeli acindezele eyalokho 
afuna ukukuzwa. Abanye njalo kabanandaba nakho konke 
lokhu, bavele bakhethe ukuzilalela, khona behleli. Yadweba njalo 
inkunzimalanga yakwabo, intweza phezu kwamazwe ase-Afrika 
asogwini lolwandlekazi i-Atlantic Ocean, iphikelele eNtshonalanga. 
Ngakusasa ekuseni, yathi cababa eDakar eSenegal. Kukhulunywa 
isiFulentshi kuleliya lizwe eliseNtshonalanga ye-Afrika. Baningi 
impela abadlali bebhola lezinyawo kuleliya lizwe. Iningi labo 
lidlalela amaqembu aseFrance. 

18 



eNew York. Bashesha ukubonana benoNqoba, bathakaselana 
sengathi kwabe sekuneminyaka bazana. Bagibela isitimela sebeya 
eBoston. Nayo iseduze kwe-Atlantic Ocean, ngasenhla kweNew 
York. 

“Stick around, I’ll make you famous,” kusho uNqoba ehlekela 
phansi. Babekhululeke bobabili. UPhilile washeshe wabona 
ukuthi ingumuntu wamahlaya imambana le. Bathi bangafika 
lapho kwabe kuqashe khona uNqoba, uPhilile wageza maqede 
wazilahla embhedeni. Wabe ekhathele eyingcuba, kumehlule 
ngempela ukulala ehleli ebhanoyini. 

Kwaba sengathi wabe ephupha uPhilile ngesikhathi ebeka 
unyawo lwakhe emagcekeni aseHarvard College. UNqoba 
wamyisa naseHarvard Square, ekolishi lomculo, ezindaweni 
zamadili e-Jazz, ezitolo zengqephu ephambili nakwezinye nje 
izindawo eziheha izihambeli. UNqoba wayethathe ikhefu 
lezinsukwana emsebenzini; bavakashe kusihlwa uma eyile. 

“Sengiyayibona le nto eyenza ukuthi abelungu bathi 
bangasebenza babeke imali yokuvakashela kwamanye amazwe; 
bazinze ngoba sebeke bawubona umhlaba,” kuphawula uPhilile 
sekuphele isonto lonke eseBoston. 

“Kona kuyasiza ukuhambela emazweni ahlukene. Kukuvula 
umqondo, wazi nezinto eziningi. Kuhlupha kona-ke nje ukuthi 
iningi lethu lithi liphuma esikoleni libe selijanyelwe yilokhu 
nalokhuya okudinga imali,” kunanela uNqoba ebukisisa 
isithandwa sakhe. 

“Abanye njalo bathi bephuma babe beqala ukukhokha imali 
ababeyibolekele ukufunda. Ziye ngokwanda izindleko emva 
kwalokho, kugcine ngokuba yiphupho elingafezeki ukuvakashela 
kwamanye amazwe. Mhh! Angazi ukuthi ngiyonibonga ngani 
ninoLynne ngento eningenzele yona.” 

19 



“Akukho okwedlula ukuthi usithande, usiphathe kahle, 
njengoba nathi senza nje kuwena.” 

Kwayiwa nasezindaweni ezabe zithe ukuqhela, sekuhanjwa 
nabangane ayesezakhele bona uNqoba. Kuningi ayekuqaphela 
uPhilile, kodwa angasho lutho ngokunye kwako. Wabona 
ukuthi izimoto zakhona zingama-left hand drive nokuthi 
zihamba ngakwesokudla. Wabona nokuthi imigwaqo yakhona 
engothelawayeka mikhulu impela nje, inemizila ngamihlanu; 
futhi ithe ukuvuleka imizila njengoba izimoto zakhona zithe 
ukuba zinkulu. 

“Akhona amanye amazwe anezimoto ezihamba 
ngakwesobunxele, noma ngelethu kuphela elenza lokho?” kubuza 
uPhilile esebona kwanda kakhulu ayengakubuzi. 

“Maningi impela nje; iNgilandi ingelinye lawo. Ukhumbule 
phela ukuthi iNingizimu Afrika yake yabuswa ngamaNgisi,” 
kuchaza uNqoba besanda kungena endlini, bevela ebhayisikobho. 

“Uyazi njalo kunento ethanda ukungixaka mayelana 
neNingizimu Afrika.” 

“Iyiphi leyo? Yisho, uma ngingayazi impendulo ngiyoyifuna 
ngize ngiyithole,” kusho uNqoba ekhombisa ukuzethemba. 

“Eyi, kodwa nami sengibuza izinto eziningi sengathi 
ngiyingane. Ngixakwa wukuthi iNingizimu Afrika ithi yaba 
yizwe lokugcina ukuthola inkululeko e-Afrika kodwa ibe ngcono 
ngezinto eziningi kunamazwe akhululeka kuqala kunayo.” 

“Kayilula neze impendulo yalowo mbuzo, kodwa-ke kufanele 
wazi ukuthi zabe ziziningi izinhloso zamazwe aseYurophu 
ngesikhathi ebusa amazwe ase-Afrika. Kuyiqiniso ukuthi alethe 
imfundo, inkolo kanye nentuthuko kwezobuchwepheshe. Enye 
inhloso kwabe kungukutapa umcebo ombiwa phansi emazweni 

20 



ase-Afrika. Abelungu baphindela emazweni abo sebewutape impela 
nje umcebo wamazwe ase-Afrika. Athi-ke ngesikhathi enyomuka 
amaNgisi, iNingizimu Afrika yathathwa amaBhunu. Wona-ke 
alithuthukisa ngempela izwe, ezitshela ukuthi ayezolibusa kuze 
kubhubhe umhlaba. Kawazange acabange nakancane ukuthi 
ayekwenza kwabe kuphambene kakhulu nezinhlelo zoMdali.” 

“Ayi, mina iyangenelisa le ncazelo yakho; futhi kangikholwa 
wukuthi ikhona engcono kunayo,” kuphetha uPhilile esukuma 
eqonda ekamelweni lokugezela. 

Zaba mnandi izinsuku zokuvakashela kukaPhilile eMelika; 
kwahlupha kona-ke nje ukuthi izikhathi ezimnandi lezi 
zinomkhutshana wokungabi zinde. Ubumnandi balezo zinsuku 
kanye nokubelesela kukaLynne, kwenza ukuba uNqoba asheshe 
abuye eMelika. 

Nakuba uMaNdelu ayezithokozele kakhulu izindaba 
zokuphumelela kukaNqoba ezifundweni zakhe eMelika, kodwa 
kwathanda ukumphatha kabana emoyeni ukuzwa ukuthi 
wathi angaphothula izifundo wasebenza khona. Wacabanga 
ukuthi kwabe sekungukubhunguka kwakhe umzukulu wakhe. 
Lokho kukhathazeka emoyeni kwelanywa ngenkulu injabulo 
lapho esezwa izindaba zokuthi usebuyela kuleli umzukulu 
wakhe. Ukuba intombi endala le yabe ilazi lonke iqiniso ngabe 
yabonga uLynne ngoba ngukudlondlobala kothando lukaPhilile 
okwasheshe kwamdonsela nganeno kwezilwandle uNqoba, kuhle 
kukazibuthe udonsa inaliti. Kwafika nasemqondweni kaLynne 
ukuthi uthando lolu lunamandla, luthi lungebonwe ngamehlo 
enyama, lungephathwe ngesandla, kodwa lukwazi ukwenzisa 
abantu izinto ezinkulu. UPhilile wabe azi kahle ukuthi abantu 
besilisa laba kabamthandisisi owesifazane owungqavungqavu 
noma onakashela indoda ngento eyodwa kuze kumbeke izisele. 

21 



Ngakho-ke wavele wawuhlaba inhlali, wanda ngezenzo zothando, 
wangayibelesela eyokuthi uNqoba makawabhekise nganeno 
amabombo. 

ilokhu ibaphike njalo. 

“He, Mrs Langa, kanti ningabathakathi yini lapha ekhaya?” 

“Usho ngani Sothole? Sesoneni ngoba ngithi sonke 

sisaziphethe kahle nje?” 

22 



“Kanti umakoti uselimele ningasasho nje?” 

uyakuthakasela lokhu kuncokolisana kwabo. 

“Bathi zingaki izinyanga odokotela?” 

“Bathi ziyisihlanu namasonto amabili. Sekuseduze phambili. 
Ezikitaza kakhulu zithi umakoti wethu uza nedabuli.” 

“Nhhi? Amawele? Kahle wena! Ngempela?” Wabuza ehlahle 
amehlo uLanga, kubonakala ukuthi zabe zimthokozisa lezi 
zindaba. UMaSishi wavuma ngekhanda. Wabe engalindele 
nakancane ukuthi zabe zizomjabulisa kangakaya uLanga lezi 
zindaba. Kusobala ukuthi naye yabe imudla buthule indaba 
yokungabi namzukulu oyosala edla ifa labo uma bona nendodana 
yabo sebedlulele kwelokhokho. 

Izindaba zokuza kwamawele zaletha enkulu intokozo le 
emndenini wakwaLanga. ULanga wazibala ngenhliziyo izibusiso 
zakhe. Wabe esesifezile isifiso sakhe esikhulu sokuba ngusozigidi. 
Sabe sesifezekile nesokuthi indodana yakhe ithathe indodakazi 
yenjinga, njengoba ayengakufuni nakancane ukuzihlanganisa 
nabantu abampofu. Wayekholwa ngukuthi babezomthelela 
ngotwayi losizi lwabo. Wayebabukela phansi, ebabiza ngezibi 
abantu abangacebile. UMaCele lo wabe eyindodakazi 
yengquphunga yaseNewcastle eyabe ingumngane wakhe 
uLancelot Langa. Ukubonana kukaLungile noNtuthuko kwabe 
kuhlelwe nguye uLanga esebenzisa ubuqidlana bakhe. Esinye 
isifiso sakhe esabe sesifezekile, ngesokuba nendlu kanokusho 
endaweni eyakhelwe yizingquphunga zodwa. Ukubuka lo muzi 
wakhe, nokucabanga ngawo, kwabe kuwuthokomalisa umoya 
wakhe. Kanti ngumuzi yini lowaya ngoba yizulu elincane nje? 

Umuzi lo usokhalweni oluthe ukuba yiqele kancane, njengoba 
lizisho negama lendawo. Kucishe kube yishumi lamamitha 

23 



ukuqhela kwawo emgwaqweni. Phakathi komuzi nomgwaqo 
kutshalwe uhlobo oluhle lotshani obusikwa ngomshini kanye 
ngesonto. Ukhonkwe ngezitini umzila osuka emgwaqweni uze 
uyongena kulo muzi. Ngaphambi komuzi, eduze kothango, 
ngapha nangapha kwesango, kunomugqa wotshani obunsundu. 
Buhle impela lobu tshani obucishe bube yimitha ukuphakama. 
Buncwelwe kahle nhlangothi zombili, emaceleni naphezulu. 
Nawo lo msebenzi wenziwa kanye ngesonto, kusetshenziswa 
intambo yokuqondisa nesikele esikhulu. Kunesikhala esicishe sibe 
yimitha phakathi kothango lomuzi kanye nomugqa wotshani, 
nawo ozishaya saluthango olufuphi. Uthango lomuzi luwudonga 
olupulasitelwe, lwapendwa lwaba mhlophe, kanti lungamamitha 
amabili ukuphakama. Phezulu luphethwe ngomhlobiso omuhle 
wezinsimbi ezicijwe ngasenhla, zapendwa zaba mnyama. Isango 
ngelensimbi engagqwali. Nalo lipendwe laba mhlophe; phezulu 
laphethwa ngomhlobiso omnyama, ofana nalowo wodonga 
olubiyele umuzi. Kalibanzi kangako isango ngoba ibhasi 
lingadlula ngokucophelela okukhulu kulo. Isango leli livulwa 
ngerimothi, lihambe ngamasondo kujantshi walo. 

Uma ungena ngesango uqonda egaraji elikwazi ukuthatha 
izimoto eziyisithupha, zime zilandelane ngazintathu. Zine 
izimoto kulo muzi. Kukhona isilahlamatende esihle esihlalisa 
abantu ababili kuphela, bese kuba wunyanyavu lohuntshu 

24 



oluwumkhiqizo waseNgilandi. Ekhaleni lohuntshu kunesithombe 
esibunjiwe esiyisiliva, sengulule ecibile, ecishe ifane nengwe. 
Lezi-ke ngezikaLanga, futhi zishayelwa nguye kuphela. 
EkaMaSishi ngeyohlobo lwaseJaphane. Yimoto esendimeni nje. 
Wayithenga iseyintsha, yaba yikhulu namashumi amane anambili 
ezinkulungwane zamarandi. Ungumuntu ophansi; akasiye neze 
unontandakubukwa njengesakabuli. Imoto yesine ngeyohlobo 
lwaseJalimane. Iphakeme, inamasondo amakhulu aphakeme, 
inesinqe esisangungu. Wuhlobo oluthandwa kakhulu yintsha 
egwilike kwaze kweqa lolu. Imhlophe, yintsha, isanda kungena 
emakethe. Yona-ke ngekaNtuthuko; akayithandeli okwala. 
Uzibona eyi-accountant yangoqobo uma ehamba ngale moto. 
UMaSishi yena akayifuni ngenhliziyo yakhe yonke le moto 
kaNtuthuko. Ukhala ngokuthi iwuhlobo oluthandwa kakhulu 
yizigebengu eziduna izimoto. UMaCele akanamoto ethi yena; 
ngenxa yokuthi ukwesaba kabi ukushayela. Uhanjiswa, alandwe 
ngumyeni wakhe. Kuhle lokhu ngoba kubandisela izikhathi 
zokuba ndawonye, kuhlumamise uthando lwabo. 

Ingxenye engenhla yomuzi inovulande obheke eMpumalanga. 
Uma ukuvulande ulubona kahle ulwandle, imikhumbi engenayo 
nephumayo kanye nebhishi leTheku. ULanga uvamisile 
ukuhlala kulo vulande kusihlwa ehlobo. Kuye kuthi cosololo 
kuye lapho esebuka ukuqhakaza kukagesi waseBeachfront kanye 

25 



nowemikhumbi. Uma elapha uzibona ethe coshosho esicongweni 
sobumnandi bempilo. 

Nakuba umuhle kangaka umuzi kaLanga kodwa abahlala 
kuwo kabanayo imfudumalo nentokozo yomphefumulo. 
UMaZikhali, okunguyena owafika kuqala kulo muzi, ubuye 
abe nesizungu esithi singamhlasela iqale phansi inkumbulo 
yamadodana akhe. Kwesinye isikhathi uze afikelwe ngumcabango 
wokuthatha ilivu ende, ukuze azihlalele nodadewabo KwaMashu. 
Selokhu kwathi nhlo umoya kaLanga awukaze ube nokuthula, 
uhlale uneziyaluyalu. Usekuzuze cishe konke ayekufisa empilweni 
yakhe; kepha akuwuthokomalisi ngokuphelele umoya wakhe. 
Kuthi nalapho esathakasela umuzwa omnandi olethwa yinzalo 
enhle yezimali zakhe ezikoma-Money Market ufike unembeza 
ukhulumele phansi, umkhumbuze ukuthi wabe ezithole kanjani 

26 



ezinye zalezo zimali. Sekuneminyaka uMaSishi abona ukuthi 
umyeni wakhe lo uyimpisi eyembethe isikhumba semvu. 
Kuyawukhathaza umoya wakhe lokhu, kepha akalitholi ikhambi 
lokwelapha lesi simo. Nokho-ke unalo ithenjana lokuthi ukufika 
kwamawele kaMaCele kulo muzi kungase kuyilethe imfudumalo 
ethile. Selokhu afika uMaCele kulo muzi wakwaLanga umoya 
wakhe ukhathazekile ngokungabatholi abantwana. Nokhoke 
useqalile ukuncibilika njengoba kuya ngokukhula lokhu 
akumumethe. Ukukhula kwesisu sikaMaCele kukhulisa nethemba 
kuNtuthuko. Wethemba ukuthi ukufika kwabantu abasha 
kuzoletha imfudumalo nentokozo yomphefumulo kuleli khaya. 
Kuthi lapho likhula leli themba, naye esathokozile, azunywe 
ngunembeza umhlebele kancane umkhumbuza isehlakalo 
sakudala eseyibhungu eligangile. Uthi ungamhlaba unembeza 
ithi bohlololo intokozo yomphefumulo. Kazi nembeza ndini 
uyomhlupha kuze kube nini uNtuthuko? 

* * * 
Wathi angabuyela kuleli uNqoba, uLynne waba yiphela 
endlebeni kuye emgqugquzela ukuba athumele kuyophenjwa 
umlilo kubo kaPhilile. 
“Siya ngokuncipha isibalo samantombazane aphilile kulezi 
zinsuku; ngakho-ke kufanele uthathe isinyathelo uma ube 
nenhlanhla wethuka uthola esaphila,” kweluleka uLynne. Wabe 
esebonisene noThobile mayelana nokuthi athathe umfana lo. 
Nakuba bona babengashadile, kodwa babekholwa ngukuthi 
umshado lo uyamqoqa umeluse umuntu wesilisa, angabi wuvanzi 
nje. Nebala kwathunyelwa kwaMnguni. Bacishe baqeda ngosuku 
lokuqala ngoba kwasala eyodwa yemali neyodwa yoboya. ULynne 
akavumanga ukudedela uPhilile ayosebenza kwenye inkampani 
yabameli lapho eseqedile ukwenza ama-articles akhe. Wathi 
akufanele wehlukane umndeni. 
UNqoba akangenanga ekhweni lakhe mhla kuyocelwa 
uPhilile. Wayisa abakhongi ngemoto, wabuye wabalanda. Emva 

27 



kwenyanga, umkhwekazi wakhe wacela ukuba akavele ekhaya. 
Linjalo iningi labakhwekazi besimanje, abakhwenyana libathatha 
njengamadodana. UNqoba waya ekhweni, kwaba wusuku 
abonana ngalo noBoysie. 

Kwabe sekuntambama kakhulu ngesikhathi uNqoba 
evalelisa ekhweni lakhe. Wavalelisa endlini umkhwekazi wakhe, 
wangamkhipha umkhwenyana wakwakhe. UNqoba wakhishwa 
nguBoysie. Kwaba yisikhashana bexoxa eceleni kwemoto 
kaNqoba belinde uPhilile okwakusuke kwangena ucingo lwakhe 
kolwasendlini lapho nje sebethi bayaphuma. 

“Ungavumi akungene ephaketheni lo; angiyithandi neze

yokungafuni ukusebenza,” kuthetha uPhilile.

Umkhwenyana nengoduso yakhe bangena emotweni baxoxela

engiyomkhethela kuyo izahluko ezimbalwa ukuba azifunde. 
Uma ezithandile, ngiyobe sengimkhethela ezinye ezibalulekile,”

kwazifanela nje. Kuyiqiniso-ke nokuthi izinhlanhla zabantu 
kazifani, mhlawumbe ungase uphumelele nje umzamo wakho. 
Ngikuphawulile-ke nokuthi sengathi wena usheshe waba nogazi

wena. Ngicabanga ukuphawula kukaBoysie ngesikhathi

oda 
ezinkampani kanye nawalabo ababedlela ngaphakathi. Kwathi 
lapho kuhlangana imizuzu engama-20 engabizwa ama-oda alabo 
abathenga bahambe, bezwakala abanye bevungamela phansi. 
“Kusobala ukuthi ezethu izinkukhu zisayolandwa ehhokweni, 
noma zisachuthwa,” kuphawula insizwa eyabe ilokhu ithi jeqe 
iwashi layo lasesihlakaleni, kusobala ukuthi yabe iphuthuma. 
Basuke beqinisile uma bethi ingane engakhali ifela embelekweni. 
Lokho kukhononda kwabathengi kwawasheshisa ama-oda 
abo eza elandelana. NoNtuthuko wathi janti ewashini lakhe, 
wabona ukuthi yabe isihlangene imizuzu engama-25 elinde i-oda 
lakhe. Yamenyezwa ngaso leso sikhathi inamba yakhe; wathatha 
iphasela, waphuma. Wathi qala qala wambona umkakhe laphaya, 
eshaya kancane eqonde kuyo inyoni emhlophe. UNtuthuko 
wafika kuqala emotweni, wayivula ngerimothi eyabe isesixhekeni 
sokhiye. 

“Ungathi vu. Ngena ngapha uhlale eceleni komshayeli,” 
kusho ibhungu elabe selimncike eduze, linwaya izimbambo 
zakhe ngomlomo wesibhamu esasingakhafula umlilo noma 
nini. Kusenjalo, kwangena elinye ibhungu lahlala esihlalweni 
somshayeli. 

“Vula isicabha ungene masisha, umnike ukhiye wemoto!” 
Lasho ngesankahlu, umlomo wesibhamu uzigqula kabuhlungu 
izimbambo zikaNtuthuko. Wenza njengoba ayetsheliwe. 
Ngesikhathi uNtuthuko engena emotweni, lathi thushu 
lagulukudela esihlalweni esingemuva ibhungu lesithathu. Wathi 
ehlala nje uNtuthuko ibhungu elingemuva labe limnwaya 
ngomlomo wesibhamu ezimbanjeni, ngakwesokudla. Yanyelela 
kancane inyoni emhlophe ilishiya ngemuva ibhungu lokuqala, 
okuyilo elabe liqale indaba. Nansiya ingena kuNoble Road 

35 



maqede ijikela kwesobunxele. Nansiya yenyuka ngoMoore 
Road yeqa uCleaver Road emarobhothini. Ithi lapho isiyela 
ngakuManning Road usho umsindo we-anti-hijack. 

“Yehla bhuti, usuphelile umsebenzi wakho. Thina 
sesiphuthumisa leli oda,” kusho ibhungu elisesihlalweni 
esingemuva, limnwaya izimbambo ngesibhamu okokugcina. 
Wehla eqhaqhazela, kuxega amadolo, ebonga ngenhliziyo 
njengoba izigebengu zabe zingamenzanga lutho. Wabe 
engabuzanga elangeni. Inyoni emhlophe yajikela kwesokudla 
kuManning Road. Yenyuka ngoBerea Road, yaphumela kuN3 
obheke eGoli. Phambili yachezukela kwesobunxele isiyothatha 
uN2 obheke KwaZulu. 

Kwaba yimizuzwana engatheni uNtuthuko emi onqenqemeni 
lomgwaqo kuduma ikhanda, kukhala izihlonono. Kusenjalo, nse 
imoto ebubende eceleni kwakhe. “Kunjani bhuti, abakulimazanga 
kodwa?” ebuza sakumemeza owabe ehleli eceleni komshayeli. 
Ubuza nje uvele ngewindi. Ayengekho amandla okumemeza 
kuNtuthuko njengoba novalo lwabe ludlala ngaye; ngakho-ke 
wathi ukusondela ecabanga nokuthi laba bantu bemoto ebubende 
babezomsiza. Sathi tshu kathathu isibhamu esinesigwinyamsindo. 
Khilikithi uNtuthuko. Kwakhala amathaya imoto ebubende 
iyoshona ngale lapho kwabe kusanda kusithela khona inyoni 
emhlophe. Kwenzeka lokhu nje naziya izinsizwa zabelungu 
ezimbili ziqonde lapho zipake khona imoto yazo. Zathathela 
ngejubane, zamqukula, zamlalisa esihlalweni esingemuva 
emotweni yazo; enye yacupha ngasezinyaweni zakhe ukuze imsize. 
“Entabeni Hospital! Entabeni Hospital!” kukhala uNtuthuko. 
Nebala imoto yenyuka ngaye uMoore Road, amalambu aphuzi 
elokhu ethi phayi phayi ikhombisa ukuthi yabe iphuthuma.

kwesobunxele kuChelmsford Road.

Kwabe sekusele amamitha ayishumi ukuba uMaCele afike 
emotweni ngesikhathi ibhungu lincika kumyeni wakhe, 
limfaka emotweni. Washaywa wuvalo olunamandla woma. 
Wathi uyamemeza izwi do. Wathi uyakhala lutho ukuphuma 
izinyembezi. Wavula isikhwama ethi ukhipha iselula ukuze 
ashayele amaphoyisa. Isigebengu sesine, ayengasibonanga eduze 
kwakhe, sacabanga ukuthi wabe ekhipha isibhamu. Yisona 
esabe siyibone isafika inyoni emhlophe, sathinta abangane baso, 
kwahlelwa indlela yokuyiduna. Asibange sisabuza, sazidedela 
zabantathu esiswini sikaMaCele, yaba yinye esifubeni; wathi 
dinsi uMaCele, wathula. Babili kuphela abantu abakubona 
kwenzeka konke lokhu. Kwabe kuyinsizwa nentombi yayo, ngoba 
isigebengu lesi sabe sisebenzisa isibhamu esinesigwinyamsindo.

“Asihlanze ngedela Nzimase, sibeke ithemba lethu kuMdali,”

sengathi ayethe angezwakala aphendulwa lawo mazwi. Iselula 

41 



kaMaSishi yakhala sengathi ithi makaswabuluke. Wabubuka 
ngamehlo akhathele ubuso bayo, wathi: “UMkhulu Somandla!” 
Washo eyivula. “Ntuthuko!” 

“Yes, how is he?” 

“His condition is stable. But there's a problem. You'll have to come 
over as soon as possible.” 

“I'm on my way.” 

“Ask for Doctor Freeman. Bye.” 

“Asiphuthume Entabeni Hospital!” kusho uMaSishi esebhekise 
kuLanga. Udokotela wabe echofoze iselula kaNtuthuko lapho 
sekuvele u-‘mother’. Kuthatha imizuzu emibili noma emithathu 
ukusuka kuGale Street uya Entabeni Hospital. Basebenzisa yona 
kanye indlela ezabe zihambe ngayo izinsizwa zabelungu. Kodwake 
bona babengakwazi lokho. 

“Izinhlamvu ezimbili zesibhamu zibhajwe ngaphakathi 
emzimbeni. Kube ngumusa weNkosi nje ukuthi zingadlavazeki 
izitho zomzimba ezingaphakathi. Kudingeka ukuba ahlinzwe 
akhishwe izinhlamvu zesibhamu. Ngesikhathi ehlinzwa uzokopha, 
kudingeke ukuba afakwe elinye igazi. Inkinga enkulu esibhekene 
nayo ngeyokuthi unohlobo lwegazi olungandile. Sesiwathinte 
wonke ama-blood bank, wonke ayalandula. Njengamanje silindele 
impendulo evela kwabeSouth African National Blood Transfusion 
Service,” kuchaza uDokotela Freeman ngesiNgisi. 

“Akuthathwe elakhe igazi ligcinwe, afakwe lona ngesikhathi 
esehlinzwa,” kuphawula uMaSishi njengomuntu owake waba 
ngumhlengikazi. 

“Kungaba yingozi enkulu ukwenza lokho. Wophile, futhi 
usentekenteke. Uma silinda ukuthi aze abe ngcono, kuzobe 
konakala lapho kubhajwe khona izinhlamvu zesibhamu. Yinye 

42 



kuphela indlela yokuphuma kule nkinga; ngukuthi kutholakale 
onegazi elifana nelakhe, futhi atholakale ngokushesha,” 
kugcizelela uDokotela Freeman ekhathazekile. AbakwaLanga 
bathatha imininingwane yezinsizwa zabelungu ezabe 
ziphuthumise uNtuthuko esibhedlela, bashiya eyabo, bavalelisa, 
bagoduka. Yize uLanga ayenenhliziyo yetshe, kodwa samthinta 
isimo sempilo yendodana yakhe. Wabona kahle ukuthi yabe 
iphansi kwethunzi lokufa. 

43 



ISAHLUKO SESINE 

Ngesikhathi ozul’az’ayithole bevimbezele abaduni 
benyoni emhlophe, uLanga wayehlezi ekamelweni lokudlela. 
Izindololwane zakhe zabe zithe ze etafuleni. Izandla zakhe 
ezivulekile zabe zisekele ikhanda zithe ngci ngapha nangapha 
ezinhlafunweni. Wabe ejulile ngomcabango, ethatha ebeka, 
akhe abuye abhidlize. UMaSishi wabe esanda kuqeda isiphuzo 
esibandayo. Indololwane yesandla sakhe sokudla yabe izimelele 

44 



etafuleni, isilevu sakhe sithe ze entendeni yesandla, iminwe 
ithe ne esihlathini. Amehlo akhe ayecwebe izinyembezi, 
ayethe mbe engilazini ayekade ephuza ngayo. Umuntu ongazi 
wayengamangala nje ukuthi yabe ibukwani kangaka ingilazi le, 
kanti ucabangela kuyo umntanomuntu. Ngesikade, wezwakala 
esethetha ethi: “Ngakutshela Langa, ngathi asiyondle leya ngane 
ngoba iyigazi lethu, kwasho kona-ke ukuthi kukhuluma umfazi, 
into engenamsebenzi. Wena-ke njengendoda wabona kungcono 
ukuthi uyibulale! Wakubona kuyinto elula nje ukuthi ubulale 
igazi lakho. Selokhu kwathi nhlo, ulandelwa ngamashwa umuntu 
obulala abegazi lakhe.” Wathi angathetha uMaSishi zaqala phansi 
izinyembezi kuye; zehla zelakanyana. 

“Uzodlula njengoba uzula kushoniwe nje. Bona abantu 
bazothini bekubona wehla wenyuka kube kushoniwe?” Wabuza 
esula izinyembezi uMaSishi. “Kangizuli, ngisayobikela umfundisi. 
Kubalulekile ukuthi ngisheshe ngimazise. Akufanele aze ayizwe 
ngabanye abantu le ndaba,” kuphendula uLanga ethatha okhiye 
bemoto, esukuma, ehamba. Nanguya eyokwehla ngezitebhisi 
eshiya uMaSishi esasula izinyembezi ezazenqaba ukunqamuka. 

45 



ULanga wayikhomba eMlazi imoto yakhe. Uhamba nje 
uyacabanga, uyakha abuye abhidlize, uyathatha uyabeka. Naye 
akazi ukuthi wafika kanjani eMlazi. Wabona ngemoto yakhe nje 
isithi nse egcekeni lomuzi womfundisi. 

“Sikhona nje lokho okungasho lutho mfundisi. Ngilethwe 
yikho ukungahambi kahle kwempilo njengoba ungibona ngilapha 
nje. Akasekho umakoti wakwami. Undodana usesibhedlela. 
Badutshulwe bedunwa imoto.” 

“Awu! Awu! Awu! Yini le ongitshela yona Langa? Nanku 
umhlaba ubhubha sibhekile bo! Umuntu usebulawa kalula 
kanjalo nje engenze nolunci? Uthi ukhona osazokuba notho uma 
abantu befa kalula kanje, befela amandla abo? Yenzeke kuphi 
le nto Sothole?” kubuza umfundisi ethukile. ULanga wayiqala 
phansi indaba wayilanda kafuphi. 

“Mhh! Sezifike ngempela izinsuku zokugcina! Umuntu ngeke 
aphinde aluzwe loluya lozolo lwe-soprano kaMrs Langa Junior! 
Akusikho ukuhlupheka, impela ngiyaphika. Akusikho neze 
ukuhlupheka okudala isihluku esingaka ezweni. Yizidakamizwa 
ezidala konke lokhu. Yimiphumela yezidakamizwa le!” 

46 



Washo enikina ikhanda umfundisi, ekhombisa ukwethuka 
nokuphatheka kabi emoyeni. 

“Kusaphithene izinto ekhanda lami mfundisi. Angisabuzi 
ukuthi siya kusiphi isitolo sempahla yokwakha,” kuphawula 
uLanga imoto isidlula emarobhothini akwa-V ibheke eTehuis. 

“Siya kulesi esiseRossburgh. Sizohamba ngo-freeway size 
siphume kuwo sesichezukela khona. Ngabanika ipulani, ngathi 
mababale konke, ukuze ibandla lisheshe lazi ukuthi kuzodingeka 
malini njengoba lifuna ukunweba indlu yesonto,” kuchaza 
umfundisi imoto isishoshela ku-freeway. 

“Kungase kube nenkingana encane njengoba intengo yempahla 
ishesha kangaka ukwenyuka.” 

“Ibandla belithembise ukusheshe linikele. Ubumkhulu impela 
umdlandla. Kodwa-ke phela ukukhuluma akufani nokwenza.” 

“Kona kunjalo impela mfundisi. Abantu bakhombisa 
umdlandla uma kusakhulunywa, bathi bohlololo uma 
sekwenziwa.” 

“Okuhle nje Sothole yikho ukuthi kazizobiza kakhulu izandla 
njengoba emaningana impela amadoda akufundele ukwakha.” 

“Cha, sengathi sibophele impela ngalapho mfundisi. Konje 
basukuma baba bangaki abakhi?” 

“Baba yisihlanu abakhi, baba yisikhombisa omapendane, 
baba bathathu abaxhumi bamapayipi. Sibophele ngempela. 
Sekungahlupha kona-ke nje ukuthi abantu laba babuye 
baqhubane ngamadolo.” Baxoxa ngokunwetshwa kwendlu 
yesonto baze bafika esitolo sempahla yokwakha. 

Balubukisisa uhla lwempahla yokwakha, bavumelana ngokuthi 
lwabe luphelele. Umfundisi wancinciza kaningi nekhanda 

47 



walinikina kaningi lapho ebona intengo yempahla ekhasini 
lesithathu. 

“What type of business are you running Mr Langa?” Wabuza 
emoyizela kancane umNdiya. 

“I run almost all types of businesses. I can even sell you if you allow 
me to.” Wahleka umfundisi, yahleka nemenenja. Lutho ukuhleka 
uLanga. Umfo kaLanga lo wawungafunga ukuthi kwabe kumbiza 
imali enkulu kabi ukuhleka. Yake yathi ukuthula isacabanga 
imenenja. Yathi isuka yabe imnika isaphulelo ngokuthenga 
ngokheshi. Bavumelana ngokuthi impahla yabe iyoze ithunyelwe 
emva kwezinsuku eziyishumi selikhokhile isheke. ULanga 
walisayina isheke, wayinika imenenja. Yalemukela maqede yabhala 
ohlwini lwezimpahla ukuthi zabe sezikhokhelwe ngesheke, kodwa 
ziyoze zithunyelwe lapho selikhokhile. Yafaka isigxivizo sesitolo 
yasayina, yanika uLanga, yabonga. ULanga nomfundisi bavalelisa 
baphuma. 

“Madoda, usekhokhile njalo umfo kaLanga!” Kwababaza 
umfundisi ngenhliziyo sebeqonde esontweni.“Ungehlulile 
singalwanga Sothole. Kanti ngihamba nawe nje ungifihlele 
induku emqubeni!” kubabaza umfundisi elula isandla exhawula, 
ebonga engaphezi kuLanga. 

48 



“Awu, kahle bo mfundisi. Usubonga sengathi ibandla 
sengilivulele amasango ezulu! Ayi, kwanele lokhu osukushilo,” 
kukhuza uLanga edumisa imoto, isuka. Bathi bangafika 
emgwaqweni omkhulu u-Edwin Swales, bajikela kwesokudla. 
Kwaba sengathi baphikelele eBluff, kanti bazosheshe bachezukele 
kwesokudla, sebeqonde ku-freeway obheke esikhumulweni 
sezindiza. Bachezukela kwesokudla sebeseduze naso. Yibo labaya 
beyodlula eTehuis, sebebuyela eMlazi. 

“Ukube wonke uwonke ubezihlupha ngokunikela ngegazi 
ibizosheshe isombululeke le nkinga yokutholela uNtuthuko igazi. 
Ngikholwa wukuthi ukhona umuntu onalolu hlobo lwegazi, 
kodwa akazi ngoba engakaze anikele ngegazi,” kuphawula 
umfundisi ebheke phansi, ecabanga. 

“Nami ngicabanga kanjalo mfundisi. Besingakahleli lutho 
mayelana nomngcwabo kaMaCele. Kodwa-ke angiboni lutho 
olungavimba ukuthi ube ngawo lo Mgqibelo esiya kuwo. Sizothi 
singabonisana nabalingani bese ngiyakwazisa mfundisi.” 

“Ngiyacabanga ukuthi inkonzo ingase ibe seThekwini, lapho 
wonke umuntu engafinyelela kalula khona,” kuphawula umfundisi. 

“Uke wayithi hloko naleyo uMaSishi. Kodwa-ke 
besingakanqumi ukuthi iyokuba kuphi. Sizothi singaluphothula 
uhlelo, bese ngiyakwazisa mfundisi,” kucacisa uLanga. 

“Nami ngizowuhlaba umkhosi ngoLwesine enkonzweni 
yomame. Angiphinde ngibonge umnikelo wakho Sothole. Ngiyazi 
ukuthi usenezindlela eziningi; ngakho-ke angingakubambezeli.” 
Umfundisi Mabuya wathandaza enxusa iNkosi ukuba ihambele 
emndenini wakwaLanga ecela nokuba kutholakale umuntu 
onegazi elabe lidingeka ukuze lisindise uNtuthuko. Umthandazo 
wamelapha uLanga, wagoduka sekuthe gidi; selikhona ithenjana 
lokuthi lingase litholakale igazi. 

49 



Udaba lokunwetshwa kwendlu yesonto lwabe ludingidwe

esivivaneni. 

“KukwaLanga. Sawubona.” 

“Yebo, sawubona. Ngicela ukukhuluma noMrs Langa.” 

“Nguye okhulumayo,” esho ngezwi elivevezelayo. 

“NguCynthia Madlabane lona. Ngisebenzela i-South African 

National Blood Transfusion Service. Ngifona mayelana negazi 
okufanele silitholele indodana yakho uNtuthuko.” 

“Yebo ndodakazi.” Seluthe ukwehla manje uvalo kuMaSishi. 

“Kunenhlansana yethemba ethi loko loko kude. Sake 
saba nalo igazi elinjena eminyakeni eyisikhombisa eyedlule. 
Owayenikele ngalo wayefunda eNkamana High School, eVryheid. 
Sizama ukumthungatha njengamanje. Ngeshwa elikhulu 
izingcingo zikathelefoni kazisebenzi namuhla eVryheid. Izolo 
bekunesivunguvungu esibi esiwise imithi kwanqamuka izintambo 
zikathelefoni. Kungaba wukuhlakanipha ukuthi niphuthume 
khona kusasa ekuseni.” Labuya ngokushesha ithemba kuMaSishi, 
waswabuluka, lancipha nedumbe. 

“Sizovukela khona kusasa, noma kanjani. Angicele igama 
lalowo mfundi.” 

“Igama nguNqoba Mzobe. I-blood group yakhe sayiqamba 
sathi i-Mzobe Factor.” 

“Awu, angake asinqobele kodwa umntakaMzobe! Sengibhalile. 
Kusekhona okunye?” Usemagange manje uMaSishi. 

50 



“Angikuyalele indlela eya eNkamana High School, mama. 
Niyochezu e...” 

Labe selibantubahle ngesikhathi kungena ucingo lukaLanga 
lumazisa ukuthi yabe isibuyile inyoni emhlophe. Lezo zindaba 
zalikhulisa ithemba kuMaSishi. Yaphenduka yaba yilahle 
elivuthayo inhlansana ayekhulume ngayo uCynthia Madlabane. 
Lelo themba lamenza wayibona isisenqulwini iNkamana High 
School. Kusihlwa zaphuma ziphumile izingcingo kwaLanga 
zihlaba umkhosi ngokudlula emhlabeni kukaMaCele kanye 
nokulimala kukaNtuthuko. 

Uhuntshu lonyanyavu lwaphuma ngesabathakathi 
kwaLanga. Lwabe lushayelwa ngumninilo, uMaSishi ehlezi 
eceleni komshayeli. Lwathi lungangena ku-N2, uthelawayeka 
womgwaqo obheke KwaZulu, walukhulula umfo kaLanga. Kwabe 
kulokhu kuphazamisa wona la masango okukhokhwa kuwona. 
Lwachezuka lapho seluqondene neGingindlovu. Yilo loluya 
lushosholoza lubheke Eshowe. Nantuya lusishiya kwesokudla 
isakhiwo esake sabizwa ngeShowe College of Education, idolobha 
lasala kwesobunxele. Lwayenyuka sengathi iyithafa iNdundulu. 
Imakwabo le ayihambi iyanyelela, ayizwa jika, ayizwa ntaba. 

Kwathi kusa nge, uhuntshu lonyanyavu lwabe ludlula 
eMelmoth. Ijubane selehle kakhulu manje. Seluhamba sengathi 
luyabukisa, kanti luhlonipha imibundu yomgwaqo ekhombisa 
ukuthi kufanele lehliswe kakhulu ijubane kule ndawo. Izimoto 
ezabe ziphambana nalo zabe zilokhu zithi phayi phayi izibani. 
ULanga wayecabanga ukuthi zabe zimbikela ukuthi kwabe 
kunamaphoyisa omgwaqo phambili. Kwaze kwasiza uMaSishi. 

“Njengoba bekukhanyisela izibani nje, basho ukuthi cisha 
ezemoto yakho ngoba sekuyakhanya.” 

51 



“Ngiyabonga,” kubonga uLanga ecisha izibani zonyanyavu 
lwakhe. Babeqala ukukhulumisana selokhu kuphunyiwe ekhaya. 
UMaSishi wayelokhu ethule ecabanga ngokujulile. Wayezitshela 
ukuthi lezi zinkinga zabe zihehwe yisiqalekiso esabe silandela 
uLanga. Ukuba wayengasabi ihlazo, engasabi ukuhlekwa ngabantu 
ngabe kade ahlukanisa nalo nhliziyoyetshe kaSathane onguLanga. 
Namanje uthule nje ucabanga yona eyokwehlukanisa noLanga. 
Ubona kahle ukuthi naye azomthola amachaphazelo esiqalekiso 
uma engahlukani noLanga. Cha, akudlule umngcwabo kaMaCele, 
kusinde uNtuthuko, aphume aphele emagcekeni akwaLanga; 
ayoziqalela impilo entsha. Akusho lutho ukuthi usemdala. Ingani 
nabelungu bahlale bethi: “It’s never too late to mend.” 

Kwabe sekusele kancane ukuba bangene edolobheni iVryheid 
ngesikhathi bebona ibhodi ekhombisa eNkamana High School. 
ULanga walehlisa kakhulu ijubane, wajikela kwesobunxele. 
Zavela izakhiwo ezinhle, ezinombala obubende nomhlophe. 
Kwaba sengathi buyabaqhweba ubuhle bazo, buthi: “Sondelani, 
musani ukwesaba.” Kunjalo, lwabe selubuyile futhi lolo luvalo 
kubo bobabili. Konje iNkosi ingabenzela nje umusa utholakale 
umkhondo womfana owayefunda kulesi sikole, litholakale igazi, 
isinde indodana yabo? 

Unyanyavu lweza kancane kuhle kukamakoti engena emzini 
ekhophoza, enyathela kancane, ebahlonipha bonke abasemzini, 
abasaphila nabangasekho. Bake bathi ukulinda kulo unyanyavu 
ngoba kwabe kusesekuseni, kungakavulwa ehhovisi. Kwathi 
kungavulwa baqonda kulo, bangena ngesizotha esinenhlonipho, 
kuhle kwesoni sizovuma izono kumfundisi. 

52 



Yisikole samaRoma lesi, abantu abathi bewuthanda 
bewenzisisa umsebenzi wabo babe bewuhlonipha kakhulu. Konke 
okwabo kuhleleke kahle. Yathintwathintwa lapha nalaphaya 
ikhompiyutha yakuveza okwabe kufunwa. 

“Sibonga kakhulu. Sesizothinta abe-blood transfusion,” 
kubonga uMaSishi besukuma. 

“Hlalelani ethembeni, uzonisiza, ulungile, unobuntu. 
Wayedume isikole sonke ngesiNgisi sakhe esihle kanye 
nokuhlakanipha kwakhe.” 

“Sibonge kakhulu ndodakazi; sesicela indlela,” kuvalelisa 
uLanga. “Nihambe kahle,” kuvalelisa intombazane ngenhlonipho. 
Kwaba wukungena nje emotweni, uMaSishi wakhipha iselula 
yakhe esikhwameni eseshayela uCynthia Madlabane. Wachazela 
uCynthia ngaloko ababekutsheliwe. 

“Ayi, sekulungile, asihambe,” kusho uMaSishi emva 
kokukhuluma noCynthia. Lwanyathela kancane unyanyavu 
lukaLanga lwaze lwayongena emgwaqweni omkhulu. Lwajikela 
kwesokudla, lwathi lungaqonda waludedela lwaciba, selubuyela 
eThekwini. Bafika ekhaya esebalindele uMaZikhali. Bangena

ULanga wadla maqede wathatha ibhantshi lakhe esephuthuma 
emhlanganweni wenye yezinkampani anamasheya kuzo. 
Kulokhu-ke waphuma ngesilahla matende sakhe. UMaSishi 
wayekhathele eyingcuba. Ukugqilazeka komqondo kwabe 
kuwucobe kwawuqeda umzimba. Ukukhala kocingo lwasendlini 
kwawuphaphamisa lowo mzimba owabe ukhathele. Walucosha 
ethukile esaba ukuthi kwakungase kube lwaluvela esibhedlela 
lubika ezibuhlungu. 

53 



“Langa’s residence, good day.” 

“Ewu, mntanami! Okwenzayo kuyobongwa ezulwini,” 
kubonga uMaSishi sekuthe gidi kuye. 

“Akuphendulanga muntu kubo kaNqoba; ngibe sengifonela 
kubo kamngane wakhe, ngathola inamba yakhe yasemsebenzini. 
Ngigcine ngimtholile. Uthi uNqoba wamgcina eseHarvard 
College, eMelika. Uthe angimfonele kusihlwa ekhaya ukuze 
anginike inamba yaseHarvard College. Ngizofonela eMelika

zethu ziyaphambana. Uma kusemini kithina kusuke kusebusuku 
kubona. Sengiyokuthinta kusasa ekuseni ngikwazise ukuthi

kakhulu uMaSishi, okomuntu ephelelwa yithemba lokugcina. 

“Ungalilahli ithemba Mama, sizomthola ngoba kayikho 
impunga yehlathi,” kusho uCynthia ezama ukusimamisa ithemba

“Ayi, kulungile mntanami, sengiyozwa ngawe. Ngibongile. 
Usale kahle.” Laphela nya ithemba kuMaSishi. “Igazi lomuntu 
ophesheya kwezilwandle liyofika nini kuleli?” Wazibuza 
ekhuluma yedwa njengohlanya. Kwamane kwacaca kuye ukuthi 
uNtuthuko wabe ezolandela ezithendeni zomkakhe uMaCele. 
Wayibona ngamehlo engqondo imingcwabo yabo ishiyana 
ngamasonto noma ngezinyanga. Kwaba sengathi kukhona 
omhlebelayo othi, “Hhayi bo, izingcingo ziyashesha, amabhanoyi 
ayashesha; ubuchwepheshe besimanje sebuzenze zaba lula izinto. 
Ubuchwepheshe sebuwufinyeze kakhulu umhlaba; usuvele waba 
ngangentende yesandla. Kungashesha ukusuka kwegazi eMelika 
liza lapha eThekwini.” Lo mcabango waphinda walenyusa 
futhi ithemba mayelana nempilo yendodana yakhe. Waqonda 
ekamelweni lokulala, wathatha isihlwathi. Waphaphama emva 

54 



kwehora, wenza imisebenzi eminingi ethi uziba ukukhathazeka 
emoyeni. 

UMaSishi waze waphaphama ngelesishiyagalombili ekuseni. 
Akuvumanga ukuthi aphume embhedeni. Laphela ihora 
ecambalele, ecabanga. Lwakhala lwamethusa futhi ucingo 
lwasendlini. Isimo sempilo kaNtuthuko sasimenza ahlale ethukile. 
Walucosha esho umthandazo omncane ngenhliziyo. 

“KukwaLanga, sawubona.” 

“Sawubona Mama. Sekuyiyo futhi leyo ntombazane, 
uCynthia. Khululeka-ke kulokhu ngoba ngiphethe ezimnandi 
zodwa. Angifinyeze indaba ngokuthi ngikucele ulunge uze ngapha 
ngoba sizokuba nohambo nawe. Kubalulekile ukuthi ngihambe 

nawe ukuze...” 

“Sengisendleni Mntanami! Bye for now.” 

“Bye Mama.” Kwakungasavumi alinde kuze kuphele 
inkulumo uMaSishi. Elokuthi izindaba zabe zimnandi zonke 
lavele lamnika amaphiko okundiza. Wawendlula ngokushesha 
umbhede, wangena eshaweni etatazela. Insipho yakhetha amabala 
emzimbeni, ezitshela ukuthi akulutho ngoba uwugeza kabili 
ngelanga. Sasingekho nhlobo isikhathi sokuthi insipho iwuthinte 
wonke umzimba. Waphuma eshaweni wangena kwezikanokusho. 
Wagaxa ithawula elikhulu emahlombe, lalengela esifubeni. 
Wahlala phambi kwesibuko esikhulu, waziphophotha esheshisa. 
Wasonga ithawula, walibeka endaweni yalo. Waqonda esibukweni 
eside, wazibuka macala wonke; waphinda wazilungilungisa. 
Waphinda wazibuka macala wonke, weneliseka. Cha, 
wayekhethile umfo kaLanga. Yayimi kahle imanzi yakhe, ikhanya 

55 



ngebala, ilingene ngomzimba, ilishiyile igabade. Yayinganqoba 
kalula emncintiswaneni wezitho. Yayisho ngothotho lwamazinyo 
anetsako elincane. Usizi lwalezo zinsuku lwase luwancishe 
ilungelo lokubonwa yilanga lawo mazinyo emanzi kaLanga. 
Akukho owawungakusola kulobuya buso. Imanzi kaLanga le 
wawungeke usho ukuthi yabe isiyihlanganisile iminyaka yobudala 
engama-62 ngoba yabe inesigubo esihle kakhulu; kuyile nhlobo 
eguga nobuhle bayo. 

“NguCynthia okhulumayo. Sawubona.” 

“Sawubona Mntanami. Ngiyaxolisa ngane yami; ngisuke 
ngagajwa yinjabulo, ngangabe ngisayibuza indlela eza lapho,” 
kuxolisa uMaSishi enamahlonyana. 

“Bengithi umama uyayazi, ngizwa esheshe evalelisa 
ngisazochaza. Thatha ipeni nephepha Ma, ukuze ungaduki. Kona 
kuyindawo ethe ukucasha kancane.” Wachaza ngesikhulu isineke 
lesi uCynthia. 

“Ngiyocela uphinde ungishayele Ma uma kwenzeka uduka,” 
kuphetha uCynthia. 

“Ngizokwenza kanjalo Ngane yami. Ngibonge kakhulu. 
Usale.” 

UMaSishi wehla izitebhisi zakwakhe eseyidambise kakhulu 
intokozo eyabe icishe yamlethela umsangano. Wathi angafika 
emotweni yakhe, wabheka umoya emasondweni, amanzi kanye 
nowoyela. Nakuba kuyinto okufanele yenziwe yibo bonke 
abashayeli lena, kodwa uMaSishi wayezama ukwehlisa amaphaphu 
ngayo. Wadumisa imoto, wathi ungenyuka kahle uwoyela 
zaya. Wadlula eGateway, wangena ku-N2 obheke eningizimu. 

56 



Wakuqaphela nokuthi ahambe ngesivinini esisemthethweni. 
Nanguya echezukela emgwaqweni obheke eMaritzburg. Wayishiya 
kwesobunxele iPavilion, esentweza ngo-N3 ephikelele ePinetown. 
Wathi angadlula ngaphansi kwebhuloho elilandela elasePavilion, 
waqala ukuncika kwesobunxele. Umgwaqo usuya ngokwehlela 
manje. Nansiya iCowies Hill ngaphesheya, kwesokudla. Hha, 
nansiya ibhodi, okuthiwe achezukele kuyo kwesobunxele. Athi 
angachezuka alehlise kakhulu ijubane lize lifike kumakhilomitha 
angama-60 abhalwe ebhodini. Athi angadlula phezu kwebhuloho 
eliphezu kuka-N3, abone ibhodi elithi ijubane eliphezulu 
kule ndawo ngamakhilomitha angama-80 ngehora, ancike 
kwesobunxele. Cha, konke kuhamba njengoba echazile uCynthia. 
Emva kwebangana elingatheni, alibone ibhodi kwesobunxele, 
lithi New Germany, Sarnia, Stapleton Road, achezukele kulo. 
Yena-ke akayi kulezi zindawo. Athi engakahambi ngisho nekhulu 
lamamitha echezukile, awubone umgwaqo onebhodi elithi Eden 
Road, angene kuwo ejikela kwesobunxele. Manje usehamba 
sengathi uphindela emuva egudla umgwaqo akade eze ngawo. Le 
ndawo asehamba kuyo ibukeka iyipulazi elihle, elinakekelwayo. 
Kude le phambili, ubona amafulethi ambethe intaba, asuka phansi 
enyuke nayo. Kazi ahlala abantu abangaki amafulethi amaningi 
kangakaya? Athi esazibuza lo mbuzo abone ibhodi enkulu ibhaliwe 
ukuthi Paradise Valley Nature Reserve. Kwesokudla, kukhona 
enye ibhodi ebhalwe ukuthi South African National Blood 
Transfusion Service. Yona-ke inomcibisholo okhomba kwesokudla; 
emgwaqweni oxhantelayo. Achezukele kuwona uMaSishi. 
Athi esahambe ibangana elingatheni, azithele ebhulohweni 
elingumngcingo, ezingenakuphambana kulo izimoto. Abone 
ukuthi linqamula phezu kuka-N3. Ahambe ibangana, athushukele 
esakhiweni esikhulu; esizungezwe yimithi emide. Sisodwa lesi 
sakhiwo kule ndawo esapulazi.

ISAHLUKO SESIHLANU 


Yaphela imizuzwana emibili noma emithathu imile ingasebenzi 
ingqondo kaMaSishi. Kwamlethela intokozo engechazwe 
ukubona umzukulu wakhe ayekade ecabanga ukuthi wafa kudala. 
Kwamlethela ukudideka ukwazi ukuthi yigazi lakhe lo mzukulu 
elalingasindisa uNtuthuko, kodwa kungenakwenzeka lokho 
ngenxa yezenzo zikaLanga benoNtuthuko. 

“Kusobala ukuthi kasisoze saziqonda izindlela asebenza 
ngazo uMdali,” kusho uCynthia eshaqekile. Wasukuma kancane 
uMaSishi okomuntu evuka okhukhwini lokufa, welula isandla 
efuna ukuxhawula kumzukulu wakhe. UNqoba wasibuka 
emanqikanqika leso sandla. 

“Xhawula Advocate Mzobe, ngukhulu wakho lona, yigazi 
lakho leli. Akasiso neze isitha sakho. Akakaze enze okuphambene 
nokulunga kuwena,” kusho uCynthia echiphichiphiza 
izinyembezana zomunyu. La mazwi ayithola indawo enhliziyweni 
kaNqoba. Waselula isandla. Sathi singahlangana nesikaMaSishi 
phezu kwedeski, yakhuluma inkaba, lakhuluma igazi. Izandla 
zehlukana bengayivulanga imilomo yabo. Bajikela ngale kwedeski, 
bahlangana. UMaSishi wasingatha umzukulu wakhe behlangene 
ngezifuba. Kubo bobabili, yehla yehlile impophoma yezinyembezi 
zomunyu. Yehla nakuCynthia ngoba izinyembezi lezi 
zinomkhutshana wokuthelelana nokunikezelana. Besabambene 
kanjalo, uMaSishi washo umthandazo ojulile, omfuphi. 
Wayebonga uMdali ngokuphephisa nokuhlenga umzukulu 
wakhe, kanye nokubahlanganisa. 

“INkosi ingibusisile. Noma ngingazunywa ngukufa, ngiyokufa 
umoya wami usukhululekile.” Washo esula izinyembezi 
zengxubevange yenjabulo nomunyu. Bahlukana, uMaSishi 
waphindela esihlalweni sakhe noNqoba wabuyela ngale kwedeski. 

“Kuyawukhulula kancane umoya wami ukwazi ukuthi nawe 

67 



uzwelana nathi thina esiyizibi. Kodwa-ke angisheshe ngisho 
ukuthi yinhliziyo yakho nobuntu bakho okukuthambisele 
inhliziyo yami. Angikucacise futhi ukuthi akukho okuyoke 
kushabalalise izibazi zokuhlukumezeka kukamama ongizalayo. 
Kuyohlala kungumlando ongasoze wasuleka, ongasoze 
washabalala ukuthi ngiwumphumela wesihluku sokudlwengulwa 
kukamama. I shall always be a legacy of rape.” Washo enikina 
ikhanda, zehla zelakanyana izinyembezi. Zehla nakuMaSishi, 
zehla nakuCynthia. Zazingehla kunoma ngubani osenawo 
unembeza nobuntu. 

“Sengicela ukunixosha. Mningi kakhulu umsebenzi 
osangihlalele. Mhlawumbe siyobuye sibonane Khulu.” Washo 
elula isandla exhawula kubo bobabili. 

“Sizobonana noma kanjani Mzukulu. Akufanele sivumele 
uSathane aqhubeke nokusehlukanisa,” kusho uMaSishi emoyizela

“Ngempela, ningalokothi nivumele uSathane anehlukanise,”

“Nihambe kahle,” kuvalelisa uNqoba emile. Bayedlula 
isakhuluma nocingo intombazane yekhompiyutha. Bavalelisa 
ngokuphakamisa izandla, nayo yaphakamisa esayo. Behla 
ngekheshi engekho okhulumisa omunye; kuyilowo nalowo 
ebuyekeza buthule lokho okwakusanda kwenzeka. Babenyuke 
benethemba lokuthi yabe isizoqaqeka inkinga yokutholakala 
kwegazi elabe lizosindisa uNtuthuko, kanti kuzoqubuka inkinga 
entsha. “Ngicela kushayele wena ndodakazi. Kusaxega amadolo 

68 



kimina,” kusho uMaSishi enika uCynthia ukhiye wemoto yakhe. 
Bangena emotweni, wayisusa uCynthia. 

“Phumula manje mama; ungabe usazihlupha ngokuzama 
ukuqaqa le nkinga. Yimi osezobhekana nayo. Wena qhubeka 
namalungiselelo omngcwabo. Ngeke iphumelele imizamo 
yokuthola igazi lika-Advocate Mzobe uma lolu daba 
lusasingethwe ngowomndeni wakwaLanga. Nina nisathathwa 
njengezitha. Awukwazi-ke ukuthi ungathi uyisitha uphinde 
uhambe phambili kulolu daba,” kuchaza uCynthia imoto ihamba. 

“Uqinisile Ngane yami. Yiqiniso elimsulwa leli olishoyo. Kube 
ngumusa weNkosi nje ukuthi ngithole wena. Qhubeka wenze 
ngokubona kwakho Ngane yami. Ungitshele uma kudingeka 
imali,” kusho uMaSishi ngezwi elikhathazekile. 

Benyuka ngoField Street bajikela kwesobunxele kuSmith 
Street. Wayeshaya kancane uCynthia, elokhu ephazanyiswa 
ngamatekisi ayeshintsha imizila engakhombisanga zimpawu. 

“Ungisizile washayela Ngane yami. Bengingeke ngilunge 
kulesi siphithiphithi. Lezi zingane azibe zisabacabangela abanye 
abashayeli uma sezifuna abagibeli,” kusho uMaSishi ekhululekile 
ngendlela ayeshayela ngayo uCynthia. Wayikhomba kwesokudla 
lapho ingena kuRussell Street. Yawuwela uWest Street, yaxhuma 
kuthelawayeka womgwaqo obheke entshonalanga. 

Imoto yashesha ukufika emsebenzini kaCynthia. Nakhu phela 
kwabe kusemini zingeziningi kangako izimoto emgwaqweni. 
UMaSishi wangena ehhovisi likaCynthia waphuza ingilazi yamanzi, 

69 



kwathi damu, wacabanga kangcono. Wabuyela emotweni yakhe 
esezizwa engcono kakhulu. Wathi nje lapho ethi uyayidumisa, 
yakhala yamethusa iselula yakhe. Wacisha imoto wavula 
isikhwama. 

“Hello.” Washo ngezwi okwakusengathi wabe eleboleke 
esalukazini esidala, esihlaselwe yidumbe elinamandla. 

“Friend, ungethuki yimi uDora. ukuphi, usekhaya?” 

“Cha, ngilapha ePinetown kwabegazi,” kuphendula uMaSishi 
sekuthe gidi kuye. “Ngiku-130 Berea Road. Uzokwehla 
ngaye, udlule iBerea Centre kwesokudla, uCanongate Road 
kwesobunxele. Uthi ungadlula uSyringa Road kuso esobunxele 
bese uzama ukupaka kuso esobunxele. Ungibhaze uma usudlula 
eTollgate. Ngizokulinda emgwaqweni. Sengenze konke, 
ngalikhetha nebhokisi. But I need your approval,” kuphetha 
uDora. 

“Good. Angithi ngingakubhaza, uphume ungilinde khona 

emgwaqweni. Bye for now.” Wadumisa imoto uMaSishi, 
wanikela khona. Wathi lapho edlula iBerea Centre, wayibona 
iNando’s, wacabanga ngoMaCele namawele akhe, zehla futhi 
izinyembezi; nokho washeshe wazikhuza, wazibamba. Akabange 
esawakhumbula amagama emigwaqo abe eyalelwe ngayo. 
Wakhumbula ukuthi yabe imibili kwesobunxele bese kuba 
wukupaka. Akahluphekanga nakancane ngoba uDora wayibona 

70 



iseza kude imoto kaMaSishi. Wama phakathi komgwaqo, 
wayikhomba lapho ayefuna ipake khona, wena owabona kwenza 
iphoyisa lomgwaqo kumshayeli owenze iphutha. UMaSishi wathi 
angehla emotweni yakhe wabuka ibhodi odongeni. “First Class 
Funeral Services. Uyabethemba? Bayalilandela igama labo?” 
kubuza uMaSishi ebuyise izinhlonze. 

“Nansi-ke i-casket engiyikhethile,” kusho uDora ekhomba

nokhaphethi obomvu kanye nezimbali ezikuma-stands kuyokuma 
kanje esontweni.” Washo ekhomba esinye sezithombe ezabe 
zilenga odongeni. 

“That’s unique! I’ve never seen something like that before. They are 
highly innovative and creative!” 

“Ngithe seeing is believing. Usuyayibona-ke into ebengiyisho?” 

“Friend, I like your taste; I like your choice. I’m highly impressed,” 
kuncoma uMaSishi enqekuzisa nekhanda, emoyizela kancane. 
Kwabe sekungamaqabuqabu ukumbona emoyizela.

Ibilungile, ngiyithanda le ngane yabantu. Ngifuna ukuyenzela 
into ecokeme.” 

71 



“Nganelisekile friend. Angikhokhe, sihambe,” kusho uMaSishi 
eqalaza lapho kukhokhwa khona. Wakhokha, behla ngezitebhisi. 
Bangena emotweni uMaSishi wathi qaphu qaphu ngendaba

“Ngizoke ngisenge ezimithiyo kuLanga. Ngizokuthi abe-
South African National Blood Transfusion Service basaxoxisana

nabangcwabi, abe-catering, abetende nezihlalo, ikhwaya, umfana

UDora lo ngumngane omdala kaMaSishi. Babesebenza naye 
esibhedlela. Waba yimpelesi enkulu nangesikhathi uMaSishi 
eshada noLanga. Naye sewashiya esibhedlela, usesebenza wona

“Ngibonga kakhulu friend. You’re a friend in need and a friend

bahlukana. 

Kusihlwa ngalo lelo langa, uCynthia watheleka efulethini 
labakwaMzobe, ngasenhla kweMayville Post Office, eThekwini. 
Wavulelwa yintombi endala uMirriam MaNdelu Mzobe, 
ukhulu kaNqoba. Wabe ekhona nonina womnikazi wendaba, 

72 



uThobile. UCynthia wayichaza ukusuka nokuhlala indaba abe eze

“Ingicasula kabi le nto. Ngabe kungcono ukuba ngakhuleliswa

“Akusibo neze abantu labaya; yizithunywa zikaSathane. 
Kabanawo ngisho nomncane unembeza lo. Ungafunga ukuthi 
badalwa nguSathane, wabaphefumulela umoya wakhe. Usuke

Yiso esesifuna igazi lezibi?” Zaphinda zehla ngamawala

“Kona kubuhlungu kakhulu okwenzeka. Kwashiya izibazi

umndeni wakwaLanga. Kusenjalo, wangena uNqoba. Wabe

Wayekhululekile, kucaca ukuthi ukhona ayekade ekhuluma naye, 
wamnika izeluleko ezawukhulula kakhulu umoya wakhe.

“Ukuba angisiye udokotela, angisenzanga isifungo sokuthi

“Ayi, asingakubambezeli Mntanami. Seniyothintana ngazo

NguLynne owayefake umqondo wemali kuNqoba. Naye wabe

abantu abadala, ikakhulukazi abomdabu, kabazikhulumi izinto

UNqoba walala inhliziyo ithe tsha njengoba ayethole ithuba 
lokuziphindiselela kuLanga. Wazitshela ukuthi uLanga wabe 
esevaleleke ekhoneni, engenayo nencane indlela yokuphunyula. 
Abantu abanjengoLanga bayasidinga isifundo esinje. Kufanele 
balazi iqiniso lokuthi lokho okubi abakwenza kwabanye abantu, 
kuyokwenzeka nakubo ngelinye ilanga. ULanga lo kufanele azi 
ukuthi uMdali usithanda sonke njengoba singabantwana bakhe. 
Kwaba yisikhathi eside ilokhu igidagida kanje ekhanda likaNqoba 
imicabango emayelana noLanga. 

Emqondweni kaMaNdelu kwafika ukuthi abakwaLanga 
babephendukelwe ngumsamo wabo. Umuntu obulala abegazi 

75 



lakhe akavamisile ukulungelwa yizinto. Kwaba njalo nakuDingane

imali enkulu kakhulu, kodwa wayibona ingelutho lapho

abakwaLanga ababefuna usizo. Yaqhubeka njalo le micabango

“Kufuneka sivukele kudokotela ukuze asihlole, kwakheke 
ubufakazi.”

“Ngeke kulunge, Thobile, ukuthi simangale; siye ezinkantolo,

77 



“Ayi, asiyiyeke le nto ngoba ayisiyisi ndawo. Ngisayogeza, 
angikwazi ukulala nginje.” 

“Angidingi bufakazi, angidingi dokotela. Angizomangala. 
Sesisalelwe yiphepha lokugcina. Angikwazi-ke ukuthi ngingamosa
