Washo esukuma, ethatha ithawula eyogeza. UThobile 
kwakumthathe isikhathi eside ecabanga engaqedi, ezivumela 
abuye aziphikise. Abuzange bufike ubuthongo. Ekuseni, sekukhala 
izinkukhu zokugcina, lamkhanyela bha iqiniso abe ephawule 
ngalo uZandile mayelana nokuthi wabe eyingozi kangakanani 
uLanga. Wagcina ezitshele ukuthi kayikho le nkukhu; wawachitha 
amanzi. 

Iphepha lokugcina baliqeda ngehora le-12 ngoMsombuluko 
emini. Ngehora lesibili nqo ekhanda, yathi nse itekisi eyisipesheli 
emzini wakwaMzobe kwa-A eMlazi. Yabe isilande uZandile, 
owayepakishe ngayizolo kusihlwa. Akazange avalelise ngoba 
kwabe kusaxatshenwe kungakhulunyiswana. Yaqhubeka 
imicabango kaThobile yaze yafika lapho esethuswa wukuzithola 
ekhulelwe. Wakhumbula eqhutshwa ekuseni kuyiwa kubo 
kaNtuthuko. Zabasinda kancane izinyawo ngoba bahlangana 
nemoto kaMaSishi isanda kuphuma ekhaya. Bazama ukuyimisa, 
kepha uMaSishi wayinyathela kakhudlwana ecabanga ukuthi 
babecela ukugibeliswa, kanti yena wabe ephuthuma esibhedlela. 
ULanga wabahebeza besesesangweni, wathi akanasikhathi 
sokukhuluma nezibi. Bemi khona lapho esangweni, bacela 
ukubizelwa uNtuthuko. Weza ehlinile, wabathatha phansi 
wababeka phezulu, wasiphika isisu. Waphinda wahlukumezeka 
umhlukunyezwa, ekhululekile umhlukumezi. Baphindela emuva 
behlukumezekile. Khona lapho phansi kwengubo, waphinda 
wachiphiza uThobile. Wazama ukukhonga ubuthongo, ezitshela 

78 



ukuthi impilo yabe isinike abakwaLanga ithuba lokuthi nabo 
kebezwe umuzwa wokuhlukumezeka. 

UMaSishi zamthokozisa kakhulu izindaba azethulelwa 
nguCynthia ngocingo. Kwathi noma sebeqedile ukukhuluma, 
eseluvalile nocingo, waqhubeka nokulubuka. Kwaba yisikhathi 
elugqolozele, imicabango yakhe isabuyekeza izindaba ezimnandi 
ezabe zifike ngalo. Lenyuka ngokushesha ithemba lokuthi 
wabe ezosinda uNtuthuko njengoba uNqoba wabe esevumile 
ukunikela ngegazi lakhe. Abuzange bumkhathaze nakancane 
ubungako bemali eyabe ibizwe nguNqoba. Kwamcacela ukuthi 
lesi samba esabe sifunwa nguNqoba sabe sifuqwa wukudinwa. 
Wazizwa esekhuluma yedwa ethi, “Ngubani ongedinwe uma 
ezalwe ngesihluku esinjeya; kwabuye kwenziwa nemizamo 
yokuthi abulawe?” Wayibona ingelutho imali eyabe ibizwe 
nguNqoba uma eyiqhathanisa nempilo kaNtuthuko. Cha, 
uNqoba akabizanga ngolaka olubi njengoba uLanga engusozigidi. 
Ukuphuma kwemali engaka kuLanga kufana nokuphuma 
kwenkinobho kwenye yamasudi akhe, into angayibuyisela kalula 
nje. Wacabanga nangomsebenzi owabe sewenziwe nguCynthia. 
Kwawuthokomalisa kakhulu umoya wakhe ukubona ukuthi 
kanti emhlabeni lapha basekhona abantu abanobuntu. Le 
ngane yabantu isizihluphe kakhulu ngalo mndeni wakwaLanga; 
izihluphe sengathi iyisihlobo sakhona esikhulu. Wazitshela 
ukuthi kwakuyothi lapho esesindile uNtuthuko, yena wakoSishi 
ayithengele isipho esihle le ngane yabantu. 

Yabuye yadamba leya ntokozo kaMaSishi lapho esecabanga 
ukuthi wabe ezolwethula kanjani kuLanga udaba lwegazi 
likaNqoba. Ukuchaza udaba kwabe kuzoliveza obala iqiniso 

79 



lokuthi kanti wabe engafanga lowaya mfanyana ayembiza 
ngezibi ayengazimisele ukuzondla yena wakoLanga. Ngayizolo, 
uMaSishi wayebikele uLanga ukuthi umnikazi wegazi wayethe 
usazocabanga. Wayethe impendulo babezoyithola ngakusasa 
ekuseni kwabeSouth African National Blood Transfusion Service. 
Enze njani njengoba isifikile impendulo? Ayethule kuLanga 
njengoba injalo? Ayi, lokho kuzomenza aqhoshe uLanga athi: 
“Ngathini-ke kuwena? Angishongo ukuthi abantu banamanga? 
Angithi awukholwanga uma ngithi angizange ngiyibulale leyo 
ngane?” 

Akazange ahluphe ngenkithinkithi yemibuzo uLanga 
ngesikhathi esehhovisi likaLynne. Wafunda isivumelwano, 
wasisayina. Umabhalane kaLynne wasayina njengofakazi. ULynne 
washayela uNqoba ucingo emazisa. 

“Usesayinile. Ngizogoduka naso isivumelwano. Dlula ekhaya 

usayine nawe.” 

“Kalula kanjalo nje? Akazange acele ukuba kwehliswe imali?” 
“Cha, akazange. Ngicabanga ukuthi imali kayisiyo nakancane 
inkinga kulowaya muntu. Ubelokhu ebalise njalo ngendodana 
yakhe okungukuphela kwayo. Uma ngibuka nje ubengayikhokha 
nengaphezulu kwale oyibizile. Ubukeka ekhathazeke kakhulu 

80 



ngendodana yakhe. Sengathi akanandaba kangako nemali,” 
kuchaza uLynne ejabuliswa wukuthi izinto zabe zihambe 
njengokuhlela kwabo. 

Singemsole kangako uNqoba ngokugagamela kakhulu 
ekuthuthukiseni izinga lempilo yakubo. Bavamise ukwenza 
njengaye abakhule behlupheka, besonga ukuthi bayothi 
bangathola ithuba baziqhelanise kakhulu nokuhlupheka. 

Kungakapheli sikhathi esingakanani uNqoba ebeke phansi 
ucingo, kungene olukaCynthia. 

“Sesimi ngawe. Ngiyazi ukuthi umatasatasa, kodwake 
akuzothatha sikhathi njengoba sizokhipha amamililitha 
angama–450 kuphela okwamanje. Siyokwazisa ukuthi siyobuye 
silikhiphe nini elinye,” kuchaza uCynthia emagange, efuna izinto 
zisheshe. 

“Ngeke uphele uhhafu wehora ngingakafiki. Hlelani konke, 
ngiyeza.” Wathi angalubeka phansi ucingo waqonda emotweni, 
wayikhomba ePinetown. Wafika konke sekumi ngomumo, 
akhishwa lawo mamililitha angama – 450 egazi lakhe, wabuyela 
emuva. 

81 



ISAHLUKO SESITHUPHA 

Igazi leli lihlukaniswe izinhlobo eziyisishiyagalombili. Kukhona 
ezine ezinkulu. Bese kuba khona nezinye ezine eziyimixhantela 
yezinkulu. Kukhona ezivamile, ezitholakala kubantu abaningi. 
Zikhona futhi nezinhlobo ezingandile neze, okuye kumenyezelwe 
ukuthi kucelwa abanohlobo oluthile lwegazi ukuba baphuthume 
bayonikela ngalo ezikhungweni eziseduze. Kuyingozi enkulu 
ukufaka umuntu igazi elingesilo uhlobo lwakhe. Akuvamisile 
neze ukuthi umuntu abe negazi elehlukile kulezi zinhlobo 
eziyisishiyagalombili, kodwa kuthukela kwenzekile. 

UNqoba wathi angathola lolu lwazi, nolunye olungaphezu 
kwalolu, wabona kufanele ukuthi akwenze kube wumkhutshana 
wakhe omuhle ukunikela ngegazi ngokuvamile. Lokhu 
kwakuzokwenza ukuthi luhlale lukhona nohlobo lwegazi lakhe 
e-blood bank, ukuze athi uma evelelwa yingozi libe khona igazi 
elingasetshenziswa kuye. Eqinisweni wonke umuntu kufanele 
akwenze kube ngumkhutshana wakhe omuhle ukunikela ngegazi, 
ngoba lingase ligcine lisize yena luqobo. 

* * * 

82 



NgoLwesihlanu emini, uDora wabe esewaphothulile 
amalungiselelo omngcwabo kaMaCele njengoba wabe 
ezongcwatshwa ngakusasa. Kwakungeke kulunge ukulinda 
ukwelulama kukaNtuthuko ngoba naye wabe engakaphumi 
esimweni esiyingozi. Ntambama ngalo uLwesihlanu, uDora 
benoMaSishi bahlolisisa uhla lwezinto okwakufanele zenziwe 
mayelana nomngcwabo. Bathola ukuthi konke kwabe sekumi 
ngomumo. 

“Ubuntu yibo lobo friend. Kufanele sisizane. Umuntu 
ngumuntu ngabantu. Uyazi ukuthi... Ayi bo, sekwenze njani, 
wachiphiza? Yini friend, uyagula yini?” kubuza uDora ethukile. 
“Ngithintwa ngamazwi akho. Ngicabanga lobu buntu okhuluma 
ngabo. Ubuntu obuya ngokuncipha kubantu. Ubuntu obuya 
ngokushabalala ezweni. Ukuba uNtuthuko wabe enobuntu 
ngabe akawenzanga la manyala okunukubeza ingane yabantu 
ngokocansi. Ukuba uLanga wayenobuntu ngabe yahlawulwa le 
ntombazane, yondliwa nengane. Ngabe akazolikhokhela leli gazi. 
Umfana ubezovele anikele ngegazi elizosiza uyise. Pho-ke, abukho 
ubuntu kuLanga. Ngangithi ngishade nomuntu, kanti ngishade 
noSathane uqobo lwakhe. Akufiki nakancane emqondweni 
kaLanga ukuthi impilo yasemhlabeni le iyimpilo yesikhashana, 
impilo engaphela noma nini. Sonke singabahambi kulo mhlaba. 
Uma-ke umuntu eyisihambi, akahluphi kulelo lizwe asuke 
ehambele kulo. We live in a very temporary world,” washo esula 
izinyembezana zomunyu owabe uhlangene nokudinwa. Wake 
wathi ukuthula uDora esetshisa amagama kaMaSishi. 

“ULanga uziphathisa okomuntu owazalelwa kondlwana; 
wathi angaphila kangcono wazibona esengcono ukwedlula 

83 



wonke umuntu ophila kulo mhlaba. ULanga akamazi omunye 
umuntu,” kuphawula uDora kubonakala ukuthi akayithandi neze 
indlela ayeziphethe ngayo uLanga, ikakhulukazi njengoba yabe 
ihlukumeza umoya womngane wakhe. “Uma ungesiso isigwili 
usuke ungelutho kuLanga, usuke uyizibi uqobo lwazo. ULanga 
akalazi nhlobo iqiniso lokuthi kusemhlabeni lapha, kusa kusa,” 
kunanela uMaSishi. Badlula kweyokwentuleka kobuntu kuLanga, 
baxoxa ngesimo sikaNtuthuko; bathinta lokhu nalokhuya 
mayelana nomngcwabo kaMaCele. 

Inqubo yasezindaweni ezisesilungwini yehlukile kuleyo 
yasemalokishini. Esilungwini lapha ahlonishwa ngempela 
amalungelo omakhelwane. Uqala ngokuthola imvume uma 
uzohanjelwa ngabantu abaningi. Uthi ungayithola wazise 
omakhelwane bakho. Uyelulekwa nasekutheni lingabi phezulu 
izinga lomsindo embuthanweni wakho. Omakhelwane bakho 
kufanele bazi ukuthi umcimbi wakho uzoqala nini uphele nini. 
Lokho kusiza ekutheni omakhelwane abangezwani nhlobo 
nomsindo bazivakashele, babuye ngoba usuphelile umcimbi 
wakho. Kwadingeka ukuthi benze njalo nabakwaLanga. 

Asilalanga ekhaya isidumbu ngenxa yokuthi umufi wabe 
ehambe ngesikhali. Imoto yabangcwabi yasiletha ekuseni 
ngoMgqibelo. Yafika ilandelwa yizimoto ezine ezabe zihlelelwe 

84 



ukuthwala umndeni. Kwabe kungezohlobo oluphambili 
olulayisha abagibeli abayisikhombisa, uma singambali umshayeli. 
Zabe zimhlophe zonke, zifana naleyo eyabe ithwele isidumbu 
sikaMaCele. Isidumbu sajikiswa esangweni. Baningi abakholwa 
wukuthi akufanele angeniswe ekhaya umuntu osuke ehambe 
ngesikhali ngoba lokho kungadala umkhokha omubi. Abanye-ke 
bayamngenisa emva kokuba sebenze izaba ezithile eziqondene 
nokugwema umkhokha omubi. Ukwehlukahlukana kwamasiko 
lokhu kuhambisana nezinkolelo ezehlukene, kuphinde 
kuhambisane nenqubo yomthandazi noma yenyanga esuke isiza 
lowo mndeni. Ukwehlukana kwenqubo yalaba bantu kudalwa 
wukwehlukana kwenqubo yezithunywa abasebenza ngazo. 
Bakhona-ke nabangazi lutho, abazikhohlisela umphakathi nje 
ngoba bezifunela imali. 

Inhlabaluhide yezimoto yadlula eceleni kwaseGateway. 
Yashaya kancane yaze yayongena ku-freeway obheke eNingizimu. 
Yangena maqede yancika kwesobunxele. Yawuwela ngebhuloho 
umfula uMngeni. Phambili yachezukela kwesobunxele. Yawuziba 
umzila obheke eMaritzburg, yathatha oqonde eThekwini. 
Yathi ingasondela eTollgate yancika kwesobunxele, yachezuka.

uMgqibelo ntambama. Ezinye zahamba ngeSonto ekuseni;

Kazi uyothini uNtuthuko lapho esethola ukuthi usindiswe yigazi

Zimbili izinto abantu abavamise ukungathembeki 
kuzo. Bavamisile ukungathembeki kwezezimali. Bavamisile 
ukungathembeki nakwezothando. Lezi zinto ezimbili sezakhipha 
imiphefumulo eminingi; sezinenqwaba yezidumbu. Kukangaki

intombi yalo noma ingoduso yalo? Kukangaki sizwa izindaba 
ezithi umlisa othile udubule wabulala umkakhe nezingane 
maqede wazibulala naye? Zidinga ukuqashelwa ngempela lezi 
zinto ezimbili. Uma uyisoka lamanyala, azi ukuthi uhamba 
phezu kwewa. Uma uyigovu lemali, noma umsebenzi wakho 
kuwukuphatha izimali ezinkuIu, azi ukuthi usengozini.

UThobile ukhuluma kanjena nje usesuke wakhumbula leya

Badlulela esitolo sikaLanga bethi bayothenga okwabe kusasele. 
Uyakhumbula uLanga ebaxoshisa okwezinja zidle amaqanda: 

“Phindelani lapho enithenge khona lokhu enikuphethe,”

Kwenzeka lokhu nje uLanga uyababona. Ubevele esolile ukuthi 
bazokwenza le nto, wabe esephuma ngomnyango ongemuva 
ephethe imvubu. Bezwa ngoba eseyithela emhlane, emahlombe 
nasezithweni. Babhembuluka ngezindlela ezahlukene. Babuye 

91 



bahlangana, uLanga esengene esitolo nemvubu yakhe. Baxolisa

kwelinye isenti, esebenza kanzima. Uyamkhumbula ngelinye

Wahamba wajubalala umqondo kaThobile waze wafika 
nakuloluya lusuku olumnyama. Usuku olwashiya isibazi esibi 
empilweni yakhe. Usuku adlwengulwa ngalo nguNtuthuko. 
Wathi angakhumbula leso sigameko zathi qatha qatha 
izinyembezi. 

92 



ISAHLUKO SESIKHOMBISA 

Kwantwela ezansi kuNqoba, kwaba yima ebona ukuthi 
kwakwenziwa yini uLanga angaceli ukuthi yehliswe imali. 
Kwamcacela bha ukuthi wayevele efuna ukulithola mahhala igazi. 
Lelo gazi labe selisemzimbeni kaNtuthuko, selimsindisile; kodwa 
uLanga esekumisile ukukhokhelwa kwesheke elabe liqondene 
nalelo gazi. Wafikelwa ngumcabango wokuthi baningi abantu 
phandle lapha abaphila ngegazi labanye abantu ngezindlela 
eziningi. Washeshe wabona ukuthi intukuthelo yabe isimgabhile, 
isithanda ukucinanisa ingqondo yakhe. Wavula idilowa 
ledeski, wakhipha uswidi, wawuvula, wawuphonsa emlonyeni, 
wawumunyunga ngesineke ecabanga. Ngesikade, wathinta uLynne 
ngocingo, wamazisa ukuthi wabe ebenze iziphukuphuku uLanga. 

“Kanti weyisa kangaka lo muntu! Usenza izilima phezu 
kokuba sesimsize kangaka! Akusiye umuntu lo, wuSathane uqobo 

93 



lwakhe. Akazi nakancane ukuthi uqondene nobani. Ngizomfaka 
emthethweni lo mlisa. Uyathanda akathandi, uzoyikhokha le 
mali. Uzoyikhokha isinezindleko zasenkantolo. Ngizombhalela 
incwadi evuthayo lo mlisa. Uhamba ekwenza kumlungela; ufike 
ekugcineni namhlanje,” kuthetha uLynne edinwe kuvevezela 
izindebe zomlomo. 

Incwadi kaLynne yahanjiswa ngakusasa kuLanga. Kwenziwa 
isiqiniseko sokuthi uyayisayinela. Yabe imnqumele ugwayi katiki 
ithi akakhokhe zingakapheli izinsuku eziyisikhombisa. Yamazisa 
nokuthi uma engakwenzi lokho sekuyohlanganwa enkantolo. 
Walibona lilihle kakhulu leli cala uLynne njengoba uLanga wabe 
esisayinile isivumelwano. Wazitshela ukuthi babezokudla impahla 
kaLanga uma ayephetha ngokungafuni ukukhokha. 

ULynne noNqoba babengazi ukuthi naye uLanga wabe 
ebavivela ngale. Inkukhu kwakufanele iwusole umgqakazo 
ngesikhathi uLanga evuma kalula ukukhokha uhhafu wesigidi 
samarandi. Kabalinakanga neqiniso lokuthi iningi losomabhizinisi 
kalizwani nhlobo nokukhokha; lifuna imali ize kulona kuphela. 

ULanga wathi angasayina ukuthi uyitholile incwadi 
kaLynne eyabe imnqumela ugwayi katiki, waphuma kwakhe 
ehamba ngesilahlamatende. Wayefake ikepisi nezibuko zelanga. 
Kwakungelula ukumbona, ngaphandle-ke uma wawuvele uyazi 

94 



imoto yakhe. Ihembe elinemikhono emide, elimabhanqubhanqu 
lalimenza abukeke eyihumusha elidala. Mhlawumbe wayevele 
efuna ukubukeka kanjalo ngoba wabe eyobonana nomhuqa 
wesigebengu. Ziyahlupha kodwa ezinye izinto ngokungafuni 
ukuphuma egazini lomuntu. Usekhulile lo mnumzane njengoba 
esanda kuhlanganisa iminyaka yobudala engama-67. Ubukeka 
ehloniphekile, usulekile, ubukeka enguye ngempela usozimali. 
Kodwa igazi lobugebengu kalivumi ngempela ukuphuma kuyena. 

Isilahlamatende sikaLanga sehla sengathi siqonde eMhlanga 
Rocks, kanti cha sizojikela kwesokudla sibambe umgwaqo 
ogudla ulwandle uqonde eThekwini, wadlula eseyothatha Inkosi 
Albert Luthuli Freeway eqonde esikhumulweni sezindiza. Nasiya 
siyopakwa endaweni enophahla ukuze sizipholele emthunzini 
omnandi. Wapaka maqede wehla umfo kaLanga. Umbhemu 
lo mude, ungamunwe ngebala, uyilambalidlile sengathi wenza 
isifungo sokuthi akasoze aba nomkhaba. Konke akugqokile 
kuyabonakala ukuthi ngokwezimali ezishisiwe. Zilukiwe 
izicathulo zakhona; ziyabonakala ukuthi ngezaseNtaliyane. Uma 
ungase umtshele ukuthi: ‘Local is lekker’, angathi uyambhedela, 
mhlawumbe akuqhasabule ngempama. 

Ayi bo, wenzani uSothole manje? Nanguya eseqasha imoto 
encane ephuma ngayo. Hhooo..., kusobala ukuthi ulahla 
umkhondo, akafuni nhlobo kwaziwe ukuthi uke wafika lapho 

95 



eya khona. Kazi angathini amakholwa uma ungase uwadlalele

Yadlula eMakhehleni, yakudlula kwesokudla KwaNdosi. 
Yasala kwesobunxele iPhilani Valley. Yawuwela ngebhuloho

iqengqeleka okhalweni. Yalishiya kwesokudla igaraji likaphethiroli. 
Hho, kanti iya eFolweni, nansiya isijikela kwesobunxele.

yobudala. Nanguya engena phambili ehlala eceleni kukaLanga. 

“Awu, Grootman, ubekwa yini lapha ngoba ngangithi

96 



kuze kufundwe ngako emaphephandabeni. Shaya i-fast move

“Ukuziphi izinkalo?” kubuza uStakes emva kokuba 
sekuphenduliwe ngale. 

“Home sweet home. Ngisaziphethe kahle; ngisekhaya,” 
kuphendula uBoysie sakudlala.

wazazela uBoysie ukuthi kwabe sekuvele umsebenzi othile.

mcabango, wabona kungcono ukulinda aze ezwe ukuthi wabe

elethe ezithini uStakes. ULanga wayecabanga ukuthi umsebenzi

“Ngabe ungizalile Nzimase. Sengingamane ngiphelezele

elithe ukuba lide. 

“Kungalunga uma siphuma lapha ngelesikhombisa ekuseni?” 

“Kahle kakhulu. Sengizomthinta ngocingo ngimazise

ekuseni. Imoto kaMaSishi yachezuka ku-freeway, kwaba 
sengathi ithatha umgwaqo obheke eRedhill, kanti izothi ingafika 
emarobhothini ijikele kwesokudla isibheke KwaMashu. 

“Ayi bo, kanti usungiyisa ekhaya yini ntombi ?” kubuza 
uMaZikhali ejabula ngaphakathi, ebona ukuthi uzosheshe afike 
ekhaya.

esinje? Bese ngithini-ke uma usudlala izigebengu? Abantu 
sebaphenduka izilwane phandle la. Uzothi usamile, usalinde 
izinto zokuhamba, kuvele kukhale iselula yakho. Uyothi usathi 
uyayiphendula kuthi thushu okungumfana; ukuzwe sekuyifuna

ngomkhulu ushova lo. Izwe selifile MaZikhali. Akusesiyo

“Kunetohwana engilitholelwe ngumngane wami.”

Baqonda endaweni eqashisa izimoto. UNqoba waqasha ezimbili

wathatha izipopolo zakhe ezithatha into ekude ziyisondeze eduze. 
Bahamba ibanga elide nje impela belandela amasondo ezinkomo. 
Umakhelwane wabe elokhu esebenzisa izipopolo zakhe. Emva 
kwamahora amane besendleleni, umakhelwane wazibona 
ngezipopolo zakhe izinkomo.

wezinkomo emagange, ekhangeza izipopolo. Athi angazifaka 
abheke lapho kwabe kukhombe khona umakhelwane.

izinkomo zami,” kwethuka umnikazi wezinkomo. Akhulumele 
phansi esethethisa umlamu wakhe; nakhu phela izipopolo 
sezimenze wabukeka eseduze. “Kodwa mlamu wami usuyenzelani 
into embi kanje? Ucabanga ukuthi uzothini udadewenu uma ezwa 
ngale nto osuyenzile?” 

UBoysie wawubuka ngezipopolo umuzi kaLanga waze wadela. 
Wayewubuka kahle ekhululekile njengoba iningi labanikazi 
bemizi labe lisemsebenzini. Wayibona nendawo ayezocasha kuyo 

107 



lapho eselungiselela ukuyogadla kuLanga. Wabuye wazidlulisa 
ngakuwo enza sengathi wabe ezibukela ubuhle bemizi. 

UNqoba akazange alubhade ehhovisi. Wafonela intombazane 
yekhompiyutha wayitshela ukuthi wabe ethathwe yindlela 
ephuthumayo yambhekisa eMaritzburg. Wapaka imoto yakhe 
endaweni yayo, wahamba phansi eselanda imoto abe eyiqashile. 
Wabe edukisa umkhondo ukuze umuntu obona imoto 
acabange ukuthi ukhona, akaye ndawo. Wathi angayithola 
imoto yokuqashwa wayikhomba ePavilion. Wathenga ihembe 
lokuphola, elikathayi, amasokisi, ithawula lokugeza, umuthi 

108 



wokuxubha, isixubho kanye nezinye izintwana ezincane. Wabuye 
wacabanga indaba yesizungu, wathenga inoveli kaFrederick 
Forsythe esihloko sayo sithi The Day of The Jackal. Wathi 
angaphuma ePavilion, imoto wayikhomba ku-N2 eselibhekise 
eHluhluwe Game Reserve. Wahamba ngawo umzila owake 
wahamba inyoni emhlophe; kodwa-ke yena wayengakwazi 
lokho, nayo engayazi. Wakhumbula amazwi kanina uThobile 
ngesikhathi ethi kuyingozi ukumpintshela umuntu ekhoneni. 
Wakubona kube ngumusa woMdali ukuthi kube nguBoysie 
othunywa ukuba azombulala. Ukuba kwakuthunywe omunye 
nje umuntu ngabe sekuphelile njalo ngaye. Walubona luluncane 
untwentwesana olungumncele phakathi kokufa nokuphila. Imoto 
yabe isiyodlula KwaMbonambi ngesikhathi ezama ukuziphumuza 
kule micabango eyabe imshayisa ngovalo kubande amathumbu. 
Wavula umsakazo emotweni wazama ukuthola isiteshi esabe 
sinomculo ozwana naye. Wasithola maqede wathi ukuwenyusa 
kancane umsindo. Yantweza njalo imoto yaze yayongena 
eHluhluwe. Wabe ezizwa ephephile njengoba ayengatshelanga 
muntu ukuthi wabe ezohambela kule ndawo.

109 



ULanga wabe ezitshela ukuthi kwabe sekuphele nya 
ngoNqoba. Kwabe kumethuse kakhulu ukuthola ukuthi kanti 
wabe engafanga lo mfana yena ayezitshela ukuthi wabe esaba 
mathambo mhlophe. Wambona eyingozi enkulu lo mfana ngoba 
wayengase amvusele icala lokuzama ukumbulala ngesikhathi 
esemncane. Samethusa nesenzo sikaMaSishi sokuthi angachazi 
izinto eziningi ngokwenzeka ngesikhathi ecela uNqoba ukuba 
anikele ngegazi. Kwamhlupha kakhulu emqondweni ukungazi 
ukuthi uNqoba lo wabe etsheliwe yini ukuthi wake wamdlisa 
uswidi onobuthi. Wafikelwa ngumcabango wokuthi uNqoba 
wayengase abe yingozi enkulu uma elithola njengoba linjalo 
iqiniso. Kwakumcasule kabi ukubizwa uhhafu wesigidi samarandi 
ngegazi nje elingaxutshwe nalutho; into etholakala mahhala. 
Ukungakhonondi kukaMaSishi ngale mali engaka kwabe 
kumnike umqondo wokuthi naye uMaSishi lo wabe esehlangene 
noNqoba. Zinjalo izinseka zabantu besifazane, zihambe zibutha 
nezibi nje, azikhethi. Lo mcabango wamcasula kakhulu; wambona 
engase abe yingozi naye uMaSishi lo. Kwalukhulisa kakhulu uvalo 
kuLanga ukwazi ukuthi uNqoba wabe eyi-advocate, ummeli 
wasemajajini. Le micabango yathi imcasula yabe imfaka itwetwe 
elibi uLanga. Wabona ingekho enye indlela ngaphandle kokuthi 
agudluzwe umfana lo. Kona kwakuke kwafika emqondweni 
kaLanga ukuthi uLynne benoMaSishi babengase basolele kuye 
mayelana nokufa kukaNqoba. Kodwa azitshele ukuthi umthetho 
usebenza ngobufakazi obubambekayo. Babuyotholakala kuphi? 

UMaZikhali wabe engenalwazi ngendaba kaNqoba nokunikela 
kwakhe ngegazi. Wabe azi ukuthi labe ligcine litholakele igazi, 
wasinda uNtuthuko. Isifiso sakhe, esabe siseyisifuba sakhe, 

110 



kwabe kungukuthi makalulame ngokuphelele uNtuthuko, 
kuthi kungenziwa umsebenzi kaMaCele, aphinde athathe. 
Kakade kakulahlwa mbeleko ngakufelwa. UThobile wayelokhu 
ekhathazeke njalo ngokuthi kwabe kubizwe imali enkulu kakhulu 
kuLanga. Wayekubona kungukudala uchuku lokhu. Ngokwakhe 
ukubona kwakufanele balinikwe mahhala igazi abakwaLanga. 
Wabe enomcabango wokuthi leso senzo sasingase siyithambise 
inhliziyo kaLanga ibuyele ebuntwini. Wabona ukuthi indaba 
yemali le yabe ingumqondo kaLynne. Kwamsinda ukuguqula 
uLynne kulo mqondo ngoba nguye owabe ebafundisile 
benoNqoba. Akukho ayengabe esakwenza uThobile njengoba 
sabe sesisayiniwe isivumelwano, lanikelwa negazi. Waphetha 
ngokuzitshela ukuthi iNkosi iyobona ngoba yona yazi konke. 

111 



“S’thandwa sami. Uyazi ushaya nje nami ngiyakucabanga.” 
“We, uyogcina ngokukhohlisa abangakwazi, hhayi mina.” 
“Ungilindele kusihlwa, ngizokulanda ngabo eight-thirty kanje.” 
“Are you serious Boysie?” ebuza emagange. 
“Very serious. Ngiyothi ngingafika ngikubhaze. Bye for now.” 


Uvalelisa masisha nje yingoba usebone uweta eseletha isiphuzo 
sakhe. 

UNqoba walithola, kalula ikamelo lokulala njengoba kwabe 
kuphakathi nesonto, ziyindlala ngempela izivakashi. Washintsha 
ayekugqokile, wafaka okwabe kuzomenza abukeke njengesivakashi 
ngempela. Wakhipha iselula yakhe ukuze ashayele uPhilile. 
Wabuye wazikhuza eseqalile ukuchofoza izinamba ezimbalwa. 
Wabona isikhathi, wanquma ukushaya ngekhefu lasemini. Wavula 
inoveli abe eyithenge ePavilion, wafunda isahluko sokuqala. 
Uheho lwamdonsela kwesesibili, kodwa washeshe wabona ukuthi 
uma ephika nayo uzogcina engasayanga esiqiwini sezinyamazane. 
Wayishiya eyivulile, eyemboze ngobuso bekhasi ayegcine ngalo. 
Nguye lowaya eseqonde esiqiwini, eyokupha iso ukudla kwalo. 
Isikhathi sekhefu lasemini sashaya esephindele endlini yezivakashi. 
Wathi angathola okuya ethunjini, waphindela ekamelweni lakhe. 
Wachofochofoza iselula yakhe eseshayela uPhilile, emazisa ukuthi 
wabe esenkantolo enkulu eMaritzburg, eyoze abuye ngakusasa. 
Babethembisene noBoysie ukuthi le ndaba yabe izokuba yimfihlo 
yabo ababeyoze bafe nayo. Wathi angaqeda ukuxoxa nesithandwa 
sakhe, wathula ecabanga ngoLanga. Wayedalwe kanjani lo muntu? 
Wenziwa yini abe noSathane ongaka yize ecebe kangaka? Impela, 
ezinye izinto zasemhlabeni ziyimpicabadala eyaziwa nguMdali 
kuphela. Ayi, akahlukane nemibuzo engenazimpendulo, 
akazifundele inoveli yakhe. Yamdonsa njalo inoveli, waze 
wahlaba ikhefu sekudlule kancane ehoreni lesine. Washayela 
ehhovisi efuna ukuzwa ngesimo emsebenzini. Watshelwa ukuthi 

112 



konke kwakuhamba kahle. Wathembisa ukufika ngakusasa 
ekuseni. Wazitshela ukuthi wabe ezophinda aqambe amanye 
amanga ngakusasa uma izinto zazingahambanga kahle kuBoysie. 
Waqhubeka nenoveli yakhe, eyamsiza kakhulu ekuphumuzeni 
umqondo wakhe kule ndaba kaLanga.

ISAHLUKO SESISHIYAGALOLUNYE 

Eziwombeni ezedlule kwakuke kwaba khona ukuzisola ngalo 
msebenzi. Kwabe sekukaningana ezitshela ukuthi useyayeka 
ukwenza lo msebenzi wobumnyama, kodwa abuye aphoqwe 
yizidingo ezifezwa ngemali. Yabe ithanda ukumsinda indaba 
yokusukela umuntu nje kungaxatshenwe ngalutho. Nokhoke 
kwehlukile okwanamhlanje njengoba ezobe evikela impilo 
yomlamu wakhe uNqoba. Yabe ingekho enye indlela yokuvikela 
uNqoba ngaphandle kokuthi kugudluzwe yena kanye uLanga 
lo. Nguye kanye uLanga owabe ezidonsele amanzi ngomsele. 
Ukuba wayevele wakhokhela uNqoba imali yakhe, yabe ingeke 

114 



ibe sengozini impilo yakhe. UBoysie ufikelwa yile micabango nje 
uyagijima. Abanye basihlaba ngenhliziyo isenzo sakhe sokwephula 
umthetho njengoba ayegijima emgwaqweni engagqoke lutho 
olumhlophe noma olunobukhanyikhanyi. 

Elinye iqiniso ayengalazi uLanga ngelokuthi kuyenzeka 
umuntu ambele abanye izisele, kodwa kugcine sekukhalakathela 
yena kulezo zisele. Kwabe sekusondele kwelesikhombisa 
ngesikhathi uBoysie egijima eqonde ethunzini elimnyama. Kwabe 
kungakakhiwa kule ndawo, kungekho nasigxobo sikagesi eduze 
kwayo. Wawuthi ntwi uziphu wesikhwama esimnyama, wakhipha 
isudi yenja emnyama, wayigqoka ngokushesha kuwona lowo 
mnyama. Wasivala ngokushesha isikhwama esabe sesifinyele saba 
sincane. Waphuma eseyinja emnyama ethunzini elimnyama. 
Yazigijimela kancane inja emnyama isibheke ngakwaLanga. 
Kwakuthi uma kuqhamuka imoto, inja emnyama iqonde 
esigxotsheni sikagesi noma esihlahleni ifike iphakamisele isiqu 
umlenze wangemuva wesobunxele. Yabe yenza wona kanye 
umkhutshana wamachalaha. 

Abanye basihlaba isenzo sokuyeka inja ibe wuvanzi nje 
emgwaqweni. Bakhona nabaluqopha emiqondweni yabo usuku 

115 



nesikhathi abayibona ngaso inja emnyama. Inhloso yabo kwabe 
kungukulubika lolu daba emhlanganweni womakhelwane. Phela

nezinja eziwuvanzi nje emigwaqweni. Amagceke ayabiyelwa, 
izinja ziboshwe kulezi zindawo zasesilungwini. Akufani neze 
nasemalokishini lapho izinja zizingenela kalula nje emagcekeni 
omakhelwane. Ezinye zithi zingangena zichithe imigqomo 
yezibi; ezinye ziphakamise imisila sezingcolisa amagceke 
omakhelwane. Kucasula kabi ukuthi uthi uzihambela nje egcekeni 
lakwakho wethuke usunyathela ubulongwe benja, kodwa ube 
ungayifuyile inja. Kwesinye isikhathi kwenzeke kumuntu wenkolo 
engahambisani nhlobo nezinja. 

Inja emnyama yathi tshobe isithela phakathi komugqa 
wotshani obunsundu kanye nodonga lomuzi kaLanga. 
UBoysie wasivula ngokushesha isikhwama sakhe wakhipha 
ucingo oluncane, oluthambile. Walibopha ngokushesha isango 
elihlanganisa nesigxobo sensimbi salapho kugcina khona isango. 
Wawukhipha ngokushesha umshini wakhe esikhwameni, 
wawucupha ngokushesha, wama ngomumo. Walinda, walinda, 
walinda. Aqala ukuzwela amakhaza egazini njengoba kwabe 
kusebusika, futhi sekuphele isikhathi elindile. Kanti-ke nalo nje 

116 



uvalo lulodwa luyawaletha amakhaza. Wakhipha ithoshi elincane 
elingangesithupha, walikhanyisa ebheka isikhathi ewashini lakhe

Intukuthelo yamnika isibindi sebhubesi, walindela ukugadla. 

Tshu tshu esifubeni ohlangothini lwesinxele, khilikithi uLanga. 
UBoysie wasondela ngokushesha, wamphendula ngonyawo ngoba

wamdubula eqondise enhliziyweni. Waphinda wamphendula

Waluqaqa ngokushesha ucingo, lavuleka isango. Wawubuyisela 

117

kuhanjwa ngemoto encane eyabe ingenalo uphawu lwamaphoyisa.

ukuyesulela ngezinto ezinjalo. Bakhona nabesilisa abafikelwa 
yimicabango ebhedayo, yokuzidlisa satshanyana kuMaSishi. 
Laba-ke kwabe kuyilabo ababeke baba ngosomabhizinisi babuye 
bawa bhu. Kwabe kuyimicabango yesikhashana nje edlulayo 
le. Babengamqala ngaliphi nje uMaSishi enesithunzi esinjeya, 

127 



ehlonipheke kangakaya? Selokhu kwathi nhlo, banjalo abantu, 
bathanda kabi ukuvuna lapho bengakaze batshale khona. 

“Impilo yasemhlabeni injalo ndodana. Iyimpilo yesikhashana, 
impilo edlulayo. Izulu like line uzamcolo, lidale omkhulu 
umonakalo lo. Kodwa libuye libalele futhi, kuvuselelwe izindlu 
ebezidilikile, kuvuselelwe amabhuloho abebhidlikile, iqhubeke 
futhi impilo. Kufanele senze njalo nakuso lesi simo. Yima 
isibindi ndodana; osekwenzekile kuthathe njengendoda; ngoba 
vele kufanele sizemukele njengoba zinjalo izinto ezinjena, izinto 
esingekwazi ukuziguqula,” kusho uDora eduduza uNtuthuko. 

“Kona kunjalo Anti. Nami sengibone kahle ukuthi kayikho 
le nto esiyibiza ngokuthi yimpilo. Indlela ahambe ngayo 
umkami uLungile, engenanxa namuntu, ezilungele njengegama 
lakhe, ingicacisele ngokusobala ukuthi izinto zasemhlabeni lezi 
zingezesikhashana nje. Angazi ukuthi iNkosi isangigcineleni

umkami uLungile.” washo ebihlika, ekhala uNtuthuko. Nabo 
oMaSishi benoDora bafikelwa ngumunyu, bakhala. 

UCynthia wayifunda ephephandabeni lesiNgisi, lasemini, 
indaba yokubulawa kukaLanga. Wadabuka kakhulu, wacabanga 
ukufonela uMaSishi amduduze. Wabuye wazikhuza, ebona 
kungenaso isigqi senhlonipho ukwenze njalo. Wanquma ukuthi 
athi angashayisa ntambama anikele khona eMhlanga Ridge 
kuMaSishi. Wathi pheqe pheqe ibhukwana lakhe ayegcina kulo 
izinamba, amakheli kanye neminye imininingwane ebalulekile. 

128 



Walithola ikheli lakwaLanga eMhlanga Ridge, wabukisisa

kufika evela KwaMashu. 

UMaZikhali wabalethela itiye, ikhofi, iMilo kanye nethiphothi

badla, baphuza.

lamakhekhe,” kuphawula uDora emamfuza i-fruit cake eyabe

ISAHLUKO SESHUMI NANYE 

“Kudela owaziyo ukuthi abantu laba bayoze balikholwe nini 
iqiniso lokuthi amagugu aleli zwe ayosala emathuneni. ULanga 
ulele yedwa emakhazeni manje; ususele nabanye wonke lo mcebo 
abezikhukhumeza ngawo, ezakhela izitha,” kuphawula uMaNdelu 
enyiphile, kubonakala ukuthi uyasenyanya isenzo sikaLanga. 

“Awu Ma! Wakhuluma ngalo muntu futhi? Ingani uthe 
ikudalela ihayihayi indaba yakhe?” kubuza uThobile enyuse 
amakhala sengathi kukhulunywa ngento enephungana elibi kabi. 

“Ayiyidali kakhulu uma ikhulunywa uyena. Konakala uma 
ike yakhulunywa ngomunye umuntu. Angithi Khulu?” kubuza 
uNqoba ehleka kancane. 

“Ubuzani ngoba uyazi nje? Ayi, sengiyozilalela; salani.” Yasho 
isukuma, ibashiya ngempela intombi endala. 

Ntambama ngalo oLwesihlanu, emva kokuba uCynthia 
esewufulathele Umhlanga Ridge, kwangena ucingo lommeli 
kaLanga efuna ukwazi ukuthi wabe esefikile yini uNtuthuko. 
Wathi angezwa ukuthi wabe esesekhaya, wathembisa ukufika 
ayolungisa okuthile mayelana nomngcwabo kaLanga. Nebala 
kwathi kuhwalala wabe etheleka. Wabe elethe uhlelo lomngcwabo 

137 



abe ezibhalele lona esaphila uLanga. Zabe zintathu kuphela 
izikhulumi kulolu hlelo. UCele wabe ezokhulumela umndeni 
wakwaLanga, aphinde akhulumele abangane. Kwabe kukhona 
nowayezokhulumela ibandla kanye nowayezokhulumela 
osomabhizinisi. ULanga ucela uCele ukuba akhulumele 
abomndeni nje yingoba sekuneminyaka aqhela kwabakubo. 
Bazonela ngokuthi bamquze, bathi uphumelela yedwa nje ngoba 
antshontsha idlozi. Kwakungasangenelwana, kungasahanjelwana 
ngisho noma omunye esevelelwe yisifo. Kona kwabe kwaziwa 
ukuthi umfo kaLanga lona wabe enenhliziyo yetshe, kodwa 
babemqambela mayelana namakhathakhathana. Kwabe 
sekuneminyaka lwenziwa lolu hlelo lomngcwabo kaLanga. 
Kwabe sekwenzeke kabili ukuthi kushone umuntu owabe 
esohlelweni, likhishwe igama lakhe, kufakwe igama lomuntu 
osaphila. Umfo kaLanga lona wabe ezibhalele nomlando wempilo 
yakhe, wazikhethela neciko elabe lizocikoza ngawo seliwufunda. 
Lokho wabe ekwenzela izintatheli, efuna zibhale amaqiniso, 
hhayi ezikuqagelayo. Umlando wakhe wabe uthe ukuba mude 
kunokwejwayelekile; ugxile kwezamabhizinisi. Wabe ufinyeziwe 
owabe ubhalwe kwelinye lamakhasi ohlelo, umude owafundwa 
yiciko. Kwabe kukhona nesithombe sakhe ayesikhethele ukuba 
sifakwe ekhasini langaphandle. ULanga wabe ekubhale phansi 
konke abe efuna kwenziwe emngcwabeni wakhe. Wabe ekucacisile 
ukuthi angabokhanyiswa amakhandlela; kungahlali muntu 
emakhandleleni, futhi angazilelwa. 

138 



iyoze ibe ngoLwesithathu. Kwafika emqondweni kaMaSishi 
ukuba azise uNqoba mayelana nomngcwabo kamkhulu wakhe 
uLanga. Wabona kufanele ukuba amazise njengoba naye wabe 
eyigazi lakwaLanga. UNqoba wathembisa ukufika enkonzweni 
yokuphelezela uLanga njengoba yabe izothatha ihora elilodwa 
kuphela. 

“Ayi bo Ma! Imoto enjena ishayelwe yimi?” kubabaza uCynthia 
ethukile. 

“Angithi unazo izincwadi zokushayela?” 

“Yebo Ma, nginazo.” 

“Uzoyishayela-ke nalena. Ake nithi qu eGateway friend, 
yikhona ezoke athi ukuzejwayeza inyoni emhlophe. Seniyobuya 
nalokhu,” kuphetha uMaSishi enika uDora ipheshana 
elabe linohla lwezinto ezabe zizothengwa. Wamnika nemali 
ababezothenga ngayo. Ukhiye wenyoni emhlophe wawunika 
uCynthia maqede wenyuka ngezitebhisi. Bangena emotweni 
oDora benoCynthia, yasuka isibheke eGateway. Babuya 
eseyejwayele kahle uCynthia, esebuzwe kahle nobumnandi bayo. 
Yabe iphakeme, inyelela, iwubukhosi bodwa. 

139 



Isidumbu sikaLanga kasilalanga ekhaya njengoba naye wabe 
efe ngesikhali njengaye uMaCele. Safika ekuseni ngemoto eyabe 
iphelezelwa ngezimbili ezabe zizothwala umndeni. Zonke zabe 
zinombala oyisiliva, kungezakwaDoves.

abambalwa emva kwabo. Amehlo kaNqoba athi njo kuNtuthuko. 
Wambukisisa lo mlisa owahlukumeza unina uThobile 
ngokumdlwengula, yena waba ngumphumela waleso sigameko. 
Laqala phansi ifundululu lentukuthelo. 

Umfundisi wathandaza, kwalandela umculo wogubhu. 
Washolo phansi, kwafundwa umlando wempilo kamufi phezu 
kwawo. Owafundwa wabe umude ngokuphindwe kane kunalowo 
owabe ubhalwe ohlelweni. Emva kokufundwa komlando 
kwalandela izinkulumo okwabe kubhalwe phansi ukuthi zingeqi 
emizuzwini emihlanu inkulumo ngayinye. Kwalandela inkonzo 
eyaba mfuphi, yadla ngokushuba. Zaba mbili izimemezelo, 
zethulwa ngumfundisi: 

“Sesizophuma lapha siqhubeke ngoFirst Avenue size siyoxhuma 
ku-Epsom Road. Phambili siyojikela kwesobunxele singene 
ku-Old Fort Road. Siyoqhubeka ngaye njalo size siyolunguza 
olwandle. Siyojikela kwesobunxele kuSnel Parade. Siyopaka 
phambi kwehhotela lokuqala kwesobunxele, lapho siyothola khona 

141 



itiye. AbakwaLanga bayasicela ukuthi sidlule khona sonke ngoba 
silungiselwe. Isidumbu sikaLanga sizosishiya khona lapha ngoba 
sizolothiswa ntambama, sekukhona umndeni wodwa.” Wathi 
angasho izimemezelo wenza isibusiso, esaxhunywa wumculo 
wogubhu. UCele walivula ibhokisi lomlingani wakhe, wabonwa. 
Wadlula kulona noNqoba esafuna ukubona lo muntu owaze 
wazama kabili ukubulala ingane eyigazi lakhe, kodwa wehluleka 
kabili, kwagcina kufe yena. Wayibuka isithule leya ndoda eyabe 
igqokiswe isudi empunga nehembe elimhlophe, nothayi owabe 
unemigqa emincane empunga nemincane emhlophe. Izinwele

zigegiwe, kwasuswa izinwedlana ezabe zimhloshana. Wacishe 
waphela uhhafu womzuzu uNqoba ebuka isidumbu sale ndoda. 
Wanikina ikhanda, wadlula. UMaSishi benoCynthia bakuqaphela 
okwabe kwenzeka. Balukhumbula kanye kanye loluya lusuku mhla 
besehhovisi likaNqoba. Bafikelwa ngumunyu bakhala bengazange 
batshelane, bengazange babukane. Kwagcina umndeni, nawo 
usumbona okokugcina, usuyoze ubone umlotha wakhe. Wathi 
ungaphuma umndeni, wasitheliswa ngale kwekhethini umshini 
owabe uthwele ibhokisi. Umculo wogubhu wanqamuka ngehora 
leshumi nambili sekuphuma umuntu wokugcina. 

“Yilowo nalowo muzi unezindaba zawo eziyisifuba somndeni, 
kodwa-ke njengoba sizoshada, bese wuba yilunga lomndeni 
wami, ngibona kufanele ukuthi ngikuvulele isifuba sami. Isifuba 
sami kufanele sibe yisifuba sakho. Ngamanye amazwi le nto 
engizokutshela yona kufanele uyivalele esifubeni sakho, ungathi 

142 



vu ngayo komunye umuntu,” kweluleka uNqoba, ubuso bakhe 
bukhombisa ukuthi wabe eza nodaba olujulile. 

“Wabazwela kakhulu, mina ngangizobabiza isigidi samarandi,” 
kuphawula uPhilile ephazamisa ukuqhubeka kwendaba. UNqoba 
wayigwema eyokumiswa kokukhokhwa kwesheke likaLanga 
kanye neyokuvikelwa nguBoysie. 

“Waba nenhliziyo kaSathane waze wafa lo muntu. Ngicabanga 
ukuthi nale mali wayikhipha inhliziyo yakhe ibuhlungu kabi. 
Kusobala ukuthi uyohlala koMhlanga Ridge nje ubalekela ulaka 
losomatekisi, kanti akabuzanga elangeni; bazomthungatha baze 
bamthole khona esilungwini lapho. Wayengalazi iqiniso lokuthi 
kayikho impunga yehlathi.” UPhilile ukhuluma nje ubuso bakhe 
buswacile, bukhombisa ngokusobala ukuthi imphatha kabi into 
eyenziwa nguLanga kuNqoba. Zabe zehle mi ngesikhathi ezwa 
okwenziwa nguNtuthuko kuThobile. 

“Okungixaka impela nje wukuthi uLanga lo ubelenzela 
imisebenzi emikhulu ibandla abekhonza kulo. Kuthiwa ubesanda 
kulinwebela indlu yesonto, wafaka izibani zikagesi ezinophephela 
bokupholisa, walifakela nama-tiles aphansi. Umncome kakhulu 
lo muntu obekhulumela ibandla,” kuchaza uNqoba enikina 
ikhanda. 

“Baningi kabi abantu abafana noLanga, abasebenzela ukuba 
bakhulu emabandleni abo, kodwa babe yizithunywa zikaSathane 

143 



lapha ngaphandle,” kuphawula uPhilile sakuthetha kubonakala 
ukuthi kuyamdina ukwenza kwabantu abafana noLanga. 

“Awubuyele odabeni lwezimfihlo zomndeni. Akufanele 
kukuphathe kabi ukuthi wafika kanjani kulo mhlaba. Iqiniso 
wukuthi nawe uyisidalwa sikaNkulunkulu njengawo wonke 
umuntu; futhi iNkosi ikubusise kakhulu kunabaningi abazalwa 
ngaphansi kwezimo ezinhle. Nathi usibona nje sazalwa ngaphansi 
kwesimo esingesihle neze emehlweni oMdali. Mina uma 
uMaMnguni, wangithola kumuntu wakwaSithole, uBoysie 
wamtholwa kumlisa wakwaCele. Sashiyelana ibele kodwa sizalwa 
ngabafokazi abehlukene. Asibazi nalabo bafokazi, sibezwa 
ngendaba nje. Wena nami kasizalelwanga emshadweni, kodwake 
okuhle ngukuthi ezethu izingane zizozalelwa emshadweni. 
Angigcine ngokukubonga ngokuveza lolu daba. Bekungeke 
kube yinto enhle ukuthi size sibophe ifindo lomshado, kodwa 
sibe singatshelananga izibongo zabalisa esiyigazi labo,” kuphetha 
uPhilile. Bobabili kwabakhulula ngaphakathi ukwazi ukuthi base 
betshelene amaqiniso amqoka. UNqoba wabe ekwengule kahle 
okwabe kuyimfihlo yakhe noBoysie.

AbakwaLanga baphindela ntambama kwaDoves and Adlam 
Reid, sekuyolothiswa isidumbu sikaLanga. UMaZikhali 
wenqaba ukuhamba kulokhu. Nakhu phela noCynthia wabe 
esegodukile. Kwahanjwa ngemoto kaMaSishi ishayelwa nguDora, 
uNtuthuko ehlezi esihlalweni esingemuva. Kababonanga lutho 
olutheni ngoba basigcina sisitheliswa ngale kobhayela isidumbu. 
Bawulanda ngakusasa umlotha, sebeyowuphonsa olwandle. 
“Sengiyakholwa ngukuthi ingxenye enkulu yomzimba 
womuntu yakhiwe ngamanzi,” kuphawula uDora ewubona 

144 



umncane kakhulu umlotha uma ewuqhathanisa nobungako 
bomzimba kaLanga. 

NgoLwesihlanu uNtuthuko wayiswa nguMaSishi Entabeni 
Hospital. Kwakungasavumi kuNtuthuko ukuba azibambe, 
eselangazelele ukwazi ukuthi ngubani owabe enikele ngegazi. 
Wayefuna nokwazi ukuthi yini eyabe izoshiwo nguCynthia 
mayelana nomuntu owabe enikele ngegazi. Wacishe wabuza

ke lapho, bese kuba yinkomo kayise kanye nenkomo kanina.

UBoysie waze wafonela uNqoba sekusele izinsuku ezimbili 
ukuba kuhlangane amasonto amathathu abulawa uLanga. 
Bavumelana ngokuthi bahlangane phambi kwehhotela ayengenise 
kulo uBoysie. Lona lelo azilolongela kulo mhla ezokuba yinja 
emnyama. Ngehora lesihlanu nqo ntambama, yathi nse phambi 
kwehhotela imoto kaNqoba. Yathi ingacosha uBoysie yadweba 
njalo igudle ulwandle ibheke enyakatho yalo. Yaze yama 
maqondana nasoThongathi. Behla bobabili baqonda olwandle. 
UBoysie wayephethe lesiya sikhwama sakhe esimnyama. 

“S’bali, ngifuna ube ngufakazi wokuthi sengiphila impilo 
entsha,” kusho uBoysie evula isikhwama ekhipha umshini 

148 



wakhe. Wawuthi manqa, ewunika ukhisi wokuvalelisa. “Hamba 
kahle mfan’omdala.” Washo ewuthi shwi phakathi olwandle. 
Wawubuka uhamba emoyeni uze uyothi gqwambi kude le lapho 
lucwebe khona ulwandle. Amehlo abo ayengakasuki lapho 
wabe usithele khona umshini, ngesikhathi ithi vumbu intaba 
yegagasi elimhlophe. Leza kubo ngesivinini esinolaka olubi. 
Ngokuphazima kweso, basuka inhlamvu kanye kanye, bagxumela 
laphaya. Kwakusadlala amadolo belibuka lidamba, lehla 
libohla, linyamalala; luphinda lucweba futhi ulwandle. UBoysie 
lwamshaya lwameqa uvalo, waguqa esihlabathini echitha amanzi. 
UNqoba wasula izithukuthuku, engazi ukuthi wabe ejuluke 
manini. Baya emotweni beshaya kancane, engekho okhulumisa 
omunye. UBoysie wabe ecabanga izidumbu ayezikhiphe ngalesiya 
sibhamu. Kusobala ukuthi imimoya yazo yabe ize ngegagasi. 
UNqoba wabe ecabanga ngomuntu owathathwa yigagasi 
ngaseBlue Lagoon eThekwini, isidumbu sakhe sakhishelwa 
wulwandle ngaphandle ezansi le eMkhomazi. 

UNqoba benoBoysie bangena emotweni besathukile. Bake 
bathi ukuthula, kuyilowo nalowo ezitshela ukuthi labe liqonde 
yena igagasi. Wabuza ngesikade uNqoba. 

“Manje uyomisa kanjani uma kwenzeka uphinda uwudinga 
umshini wakho?” 

“Ngeke ngisawudinga njengoba isishintshile impilo yami. 
Yincane kabi imali umuntu abeyithola ngalo msebenzi. 
Ngabanikazi bomsebenzi abenza imali. Wena sithunywa ugcina 
ngokuthola imvuthu nje engasho lutho.”

“Kodwa ube wenziwe nguwe umsebenzi; uphinde ulithwale

“Ngizofunda i-I.T, Information Technology, S’bali.” 

“Ayi-ke, nami ngingaliphonsa itshe esivivaneni uma kunjalo.”

ningifundise.” 

UNqoba wakhipha inkulungwane eyodwa yamarandi, 
wathembisa ukuyikhokha ngakusasa enye. Babuya ngayo futhi 
indlela ababehambe ngayo. UBoysie wehliswa lapho ayecoshwe 
khona. Lwake lwamuthi heqe uvalo uNqoba eseyedwa egoduka. 
Wayecabanga okwakuyokwenzeka ukuba uBoysie wayenyomuke 
kulo msebenzi ngaphambi kokuba afe uLanga. 

Wavula umsakazo emotweni, ezama ukwehlisa lolo luvalo. 
Zaba ziningana iziteshi zemisakazo azizama, kepha ingqondo 
yathi angiyi lapho; isacubungula yona le ndaba yezenzo 
zikaLanga. Wagcina ewucishile umsakazo, ebona sekumshayelisa 
kabana ukushintshana neziteshi. Imoto wayikhomba kuSmith 
Street yadweba ngaye njalo yaze yayoxhuma kuBerea Road. Wathi 
angayedlula iBerea Centre, wajikela kwesobunxele esitolokazi 
esithengisa izithelo namaveji. Wathenga izinhlobonhlobo 
zezithelo ukuze athi angafika ekhaya azenzele isaladi yazo. 
Ukukhetha izithelo kwake kwathi ukuwuphumuza umqondo 
kaNqoba ekugqilazweni wukucabanga ngoSathane onguLanga. 

150 



Esephindela emotweni, enyuka ngaye uBerea Road, wazibuza 
ukuthi yini eyabe ibuyisele uLanga emicabangweni yakhe? 
Wawubona ngamanye amehlo engqondo umsebenzi owabe 
wenziwe nguBoysie. Wasincoma ngenhliziyo isenzo sakhe 
sokungambukeli phansi umlamu wakhe, nakuba uPhilile ayeqale 
wangathanda ukuba bajwayelane. 



23. Wasifunda ngenhliziyo kaningana, enokondisa ivesi lokuqala 
elithi: “UJehova ungumalusi wami, angiyukweswela,” nengxenye 
yokuqala yelesine ethi: “Noma ngihamba esigodini sethunzi lokufa, 
angesabi okubi ngokuba wena unami, ...” Emva kwesikhathi 
efunda ngenhliziyo ephindaphinda, wathandaza ebonga uMdali 
ngokumsindisa esihlukwini sikaLanga. Wacambalala embhedeni, 
esacabanga ngako ukuphephiswa kwakhe esenzweni sobuSathane 
bukaLanga. Wagcina ezumekile walala zwi. 
151 



ISAHLUKO SESHUMI NAMBILI 

Lwaze lwafika usuku ayelubheke ngamehlo abomvu 
uMaSishi benendodana yakhe uNtuthuko; usuku lokufundwa 
kwewili. UMaSishi wabe engenalo ithemba eliphelele njengoba 
wabe ungesemuhle umoya phakathi kwakhe nomyeni wakhe. 
UNtuthuko wabe enethemba eliphelele njengoba abe ekwenze 
konke okwabe kufunwe nguyise uLanga. Nguye uLanga 
owabe ethe indodana yakhe kufanele ibe yi-accountant. Nguye 
owayehlele ukuba ithathe uMaCele. Nguye futhi uLanga 
owayenqabele uNtuthuko noMaCele ekutheni baphume umuzi 
wabo. Pho yini ayengajeziselwa yona njengoba ayekwenze konke 
okwabe kufunwe nguyise? UNtuthuko waphinda wazinuka 
amakhwapha esehlehle kakhulu kunakuqala. Waqala eminyakeni 
yakhe yobufana, wangathola phutha elibi ake walenza. Wadlulela 
eminyakeni yakhe yobubhungu; wawakhumbula sengathi wabe 
ewenze ngayizolo amacala akhe amabili amabi kakhulu. Elokuqala 
kwabe kungelokweqa eSt Francis College, eMariannhill, waya 
kophuza nabanye abafana ababili. Babanjwa, kwaphetha 
ngokuthi baxoshwe. Lelo cala lalanywa ngelabe lilibi kakhulu. 

152 



Lona-ke lacishe lamkhipha ngesango emzini kaLanga. Kwaba 
sengathi uyawezwa ezindlebeni zakhe amazwi kaLanga, awasho 
ethukuthele egqamuka amalangabi: 

“Yes Daddy, ngikuzwa kahle. Ngiyaxolisa Daddy, ngeke 
ngiphinde,” 

“Ungizwa kahle ukuthini?” 

“Ukuthi uma ngiqhuba kanje, ngeke ngithole lutho efeni lika-
Daddy.” 

“Should you do such a stupid thing again, I will definitely disown 
you. Do you understand that?” 

“Yes Daddy, I do understand.” 

“Uphinde-ke wenze umbhedo wakho, uyongifunda ungiqonde.” 

Ngokuhamba kweminyaka, ladlula lelo cala likaNtuthuko 
emqondweni kaLanga, kodwa kumninilo lashiya izibazi 
ezingasoze zashabalala. Umenziwa lamshiya nenkambabeyibuza. 
Kunjalo, baningana ababebuzana ukuthi kwakhala nyonini kulo 
dokotela njengoba emuhle kangaka, emi kahle kanje, enogazi 
kangaka, kodwa umshado do. Zehlukahlukene, ziyashiyashiyana 
izigameko ezenzeka empilweni yomuntu. Kukhona okuthi 
ngokuhamba kwesikhathi zishabalale emqondweni wesidalwa 
esingumuntu, uzwe nezifundiswa sezikwitiza zithi, “Time heals.” 
Kukhona ezishiya izibazi ezingasoze zashabalala; kanti kukhona 
nezishiya inkambabeyibuza. EkaThobile inkambabeyibuza 
yehlula ngisho nodokotela bengqondo. Zazikhona izikhathi 
lapho ayebuka uNqoba maqede kufike emqondweni wakhe 
ukuthi wayemthole kanjani. Emqondweni kaThobile umuntu 

153 



wesilisa wayefana nesilwane esingenaluthando, esingenamusa, 
esingenasihe. Izinyembezi zaziza zelakanyana uma kuke kwaba 
nomlisa ozibika kuye. 

“Angiqale ngokuchaza ukuthi akusikho okwami ukuphawula 
mayelana nokuthi uLanga ulabe kahle noma kabi ifa lakhe. 
Okwami ngukuthi ngethule lokho okuyizifiso zakhe, futhi 
angithume ukuthi ngizifeze.” Wathi angethula isendlalelo 
sakhe, waqala ukufunda iwili. UNtuthuko wabelwa indlu, 
amasheya ezinkampani ezintathu ayecela ezigidini ezimbili 
zamarandi esewonke. Wathola nemali eyabe ifakwe koma-Money 
Market, eyabe yanda ngesivinini isicishe ibe yisigidi nohhafu. 
Umshuwalense kaLanga owabe uzokhokha amakhulu ayisithupha 
ezinkulungwane zamarandi wawubhalwe yena futhi uNtuthuko. 
Zabe zabelwe yena nezimoto zikaLanga. UMaCele wabe ebhalwe 
emalini eyabe isebhange, icishe ibe ngamarandi ayizinkulungwane 
eziyikhulu namashumi ayisihlanu. Kwacaca ukuthi uLanga 
wabe ezunywe ngukufa engakamkhiphi uMaCele ewilini yakhe. 
UMaSishi wabe esezitshelile ngenhliziyo ukuthi wabe engabelwanga 
lutho efeni likaLanga. Esetshisa lowo mcabango wakhe, walizwa 
selibizwa nelakhe igama ekugcineni. Wabelwa izinkulungwane 
zamarandi ezabe zicela emakhulwini amabili ezabe zisebhange. 

“Uxolo mmeli. Wathini uLanga kuwena? Wathi sashada 
umshado ohlanganisa amafa, in community of property noma 
ohlukanisa amafa, out of community of property?” Wabuza 
ngomoya ophansi uMaSishi ezama ukuzibamba ngoba 

154 



intukuthelo yabe isigqibelene ngaphakathi kuye. 

“Kukhona yini okungalungile Mrs Langa?” kubuza ummeli 
ezenza odidekile. 

“Yincwadi yommeli wami esiyophendula lowo mbuzo. 
Uzoyithola khona maduze nje,” kuphendula uMaSishi 
ethukuthele eqhuma, kodwa ezibamba. 

“Ma, ngizokuhlephulela efeni likababa. Asikho nesincane 
isidingo sokuthi uthathe ummeli,” kuncenga uNtuthuko ngezwi 
elikhathazekile. 

“Ngizohleshulelwa uwena entweni yami? Mqondo muni 
lowo? What mentality is that? Kanti kunjani emhlabeni bantu? 
Angifune kuqhoshelwa nguwena mina, ulokhu ungitshela 
ukuthi wangihlephulela efeni likayihlo. Khohlwa! Ummeli wami 
uzoyilungisa yonke le nto.” 

“Ma, kuzokuba yihlazo sekuphuma emaphephandabeni ukuthi 
sesithathelene abameli sibanga ifa likababa. Uzothola noma yini 
oyifunayo ma. Ngiyakucela, please Ma,” kuncenga uNtuthuko 
sekucwebe nezinyembezi. 

“Wazini ngehlazo wena? Wena noyihlo kanazi lutho ngehlazo. 
Mhlawumbe kufanele ngiluthathe njengoba lunjalo udaba 
lukaNqoba benonina ngiyoluthi bhadla ephephandabeni 
elifundwa kakhulu, yikhona...” 

“Awu! Awu! Awu! Kodwa Ma! Usungingcwaba ngiphila, 
yize ungizala Ma?” Washo ekhonkobalisa okomuntu ogwazwe 
ngomkhonto esiswini uNtuthuko. Kwezwela kuMaSishi, 
esekhumbula nokuthi yabe ingakapholi kahle imithungo 
kuNtuthuko. Intukuthelo yadamba ngokushesha kuMaSishi. 

155 



“Khululeka. Ngeke ngiye ephephandabeni; kodwa ngiyaya 
kummeli wami. Ngicabanga ukuthi sesiqedile mmeli,” kusho 
uMaSishi kubonakala ukuthi wabe engasazimisele ngokwanda 
nenkulumo. 

“Yebo Khulu.” 

“Mzukulu, ngidinga usizo lwakho lomthetho. Kufanele 
ngikubone ngokushesha,” kuchaza uMaSishi ngezwi 

elikhathazekile. Ingqondo kaNqoba yagijimisa okonyazi. 

“Kumayelana newili yini Khulu?” 

“Yebo Ngane yami. Bengingazi ukuthi ngihleli nje kanti...” 

“Khululeka khulu. That’s my speciality. Uzokuthola konke 

okufunayo. Nami ngizoyithola yonke imali yami.” 

“Uzoyithola Ngane yami. Futhi-ke ikhona, iyizindodla,” 
kuphetha uMaSishi esethe ukukhululeka. 

“Kungakulungela ukufika ehhovisi ngehora lesishiyagalolunye 

kusasa ekuseni?” 

“Ngizofika Mntanomntanami. Bye for now.” 

“Bye Khulu,” kuvalelisa uNqoba naye esekhululeke kakhulu 
emva kokuzwa ukuthi uLanga wabe eshiye izindodla zemali.

enovadlwana njengoba babeqala ukukhulumisana. UMaNdelu

seliqengqeleka ethafeni eliyitafula lentaba. Basheshe bawubona 
umuzi ababebabele kuwo. UMaZikhali wehla kwaMbili, adlula 
wodwa amadoda. Ilori yama ngaphandle komuzi; wasala kuyo 
nomshayeli wayo. Kwehla amadoda amabili ayokhuleka. Asheshe 
angeniswa. Angeniswa nje asephelile wuvalo njengoba ezolungisa 
umonakalo osekukudala wenzeka. Nawo ayazibonela nje ukuthi 

164 



angashaywa nokushaywa. Nokho-ke abuye aziduduze ngokuthi 
wona kawonanga lutho, athunyiwe. Kona kuyiqiniso ukuthi 
isithunywa kasibekwa cala. Kodwa-ke bakhona nabakholelwa 
ekutheni ihawu liyashaywa. Kwathi gidi bebona bemukelwa 
kahle. Zehliswa izilwane, zafakwa ezibayeni zakhona. Kwathi

amadoda acela ukuvalelisa; hleze kufike isixhwanguxhwangu

kusehla kahle, uvalo lulokhu luthi ngila. Kwaze kwathi gidi 
lapho isisuka ilori, isiphindela nabo emuva. UMaZikhali wathi 
angayibona isuka ilori, waphuma naye eseyolinda emgwaqweni. 

Uma umi phezu kwaleli liwa lendawo eyitafula, ulibona 
lonke leli damukazi. Yithi ungakhathala wukubukana naleli 
damukazi, amehlo akho uwajikijele koBotha’s Hill, koHillcrest 
nakoMolweni. Ungasheshi ukuwakhalima, wayeke nje athilileke 
njalo aze ayokhathalela koDabeka nakoClermont. Kanti-ke uma 
libalele lacwatha kahle ungathuka usuyibona kahle neNewlands 
West. Ungazikhathazi ngeLindelani, neNtuzuma kanye noMashu 
ngoba lezo zindawo zisithwe yiNgqwaqube uma umi kule ndawo. 

Uma uphenduka ufulathela idamu, amehlo uwajikijela 

165 



eNyakathompumalanga, ngoba uthi ufuna ukubona eNdwedwe, 
uzidlalela ngesikhathi sakho nje ngoba kusithe ungelengele 
lwezintaba ezinjengoThelezini, oDonsumlenzana nezinye. 
Kuze kube ngconywana uma ubheka enyakatho koMqeku 
nakoThafamasi. Nayo njalo iThafamasi le yabhimbiswa yibo 
abelungu. Kona ngempela kuseThaphamasi, okuyigama 
elaqanjwa ngamakhehla ndulondulo, ngesikhathi ethi, 
“Hambani bafana niyozelusela laphaya ukuze ziyothapha amasi.” 
Ngokuhamba kwesikhathi kwathiwa kuseThaphamasi. Abelungu 
bathi kuseThafamasi. Uzokhumbula phela ukuthi u-‘ph’ ubizwa 
ngo-‘f’ ngesilungu.

ISAHLUKO SESHUMI NANTATHU 

“Kufanele wazi kahle Ntuthuko ukuthi kunzima nakubona 
abakwaMzobe ukuthi bahlanganise amehlo nawe, ngoba lokho 
kubathunuka amanxeba amadala. Kulindele nokuthi bangase 
bangavumi ukubonana nawe; noma bathi kwanele osekwenziwe, 
asisekho isidingo soxolo lomlomo. Lindela noma yini ntanami, 
yisimo esilukhuni kabi lesi,” kuchaza uMaSishi ekhathazekile. 
Waphefumula kakhulu uNtuthuko okomuntu ephelelwa 
yithemba lokugcina. “Nokho-ke ngisazoke ngibonisane noNqoba. 
Uma evuma ukuthi kuhlanganwe, ngiyobe sengimcela ukuba 
asincengele unina noninakhulu. Uma nabo bevuma, ngiyonxusa 
uMaZikhali noCynthia ukuba basikhaphe,” kuphetha uMaSishi 
engenalo ithemba lokuthi babengase bavume abakwaMzobe 
ukuthi kuhlanganiswe amehlo. 

“Kazi uyongibheka kanjani lowo mfana?” kuzikhalela 
uNtuthuko ebheke phansi ecabanga. 

“Yena ubukeka engumuntu osexolile. Futhi-ke useke 
walithola ithuba lokubhodla. Wakhuluma wangashiya lutho 
mhla siqala ukumbona. Ngunina umuntu engicabanga ukuthi 
usazothunukala kakhulu.” 

“Ayi, sekuyobonakala khona. Kodwa-ke kufanele sehluleke 
sizamile.” 

“Angingapholisi maseko, angifonele uNqoba njengamanje.” 
UMaSishi washo eqonda ocingweni lwasendlini. Wamthola 
ehhovisi, wamchazela, bezwana. 

167 



“Khululeka Khulu, ngizobancenga baze bavume. Yona 
ibuhlungu ngempela le nto; kodwa-ke ivele injalo impilo 
yasemhlabeni, kube kungekuhle nokubambelana amagqubu.” 

“Kawenzi iphutha Khulu; yindoda ongayethemba lena,” 

kuphetha uNqoba ngokudlalisa ukhulu wakhe. 

“Angikuthinte ngomhlomunye, ngizwe ukuthi batheni.” 

“Uyothintwa yimi Khulu, khululeka,” kuphetha uNqoba 
enamile. Ingxoxo yabo yamnika ithemba uMaSishi. Ukwenama 
kukaNqoba kwakuthe ukuwukhulula umoya wakhe. Kwabe 
kumfanele ukwenama uNqoba ngoba izinto zabe zithanda 
ukumchuma kwezezimali. Wabe uhamba kahle umsebenzi, ingena 
kahle nenzalo yezimali zakhe, ikakhulukazi ekahhafu wesigidi 
samarandi. Ayehamba kahle namalungiselelo omshado wakhe 
noPhilile. UBoysie wabe eseziqalile izifundo zekhompuyutha, 
ezokuya kofunda eDurban University of Technology ekuqaleni 
konyaka omusha. 

UNqoba wabancenga baze bavuma oThobile benoMaNdelu. 

“Yini sengathi isikuthengile nje le mali yegazi? Awuzothi 
usuka ube uguqukela esibongweni salaba bantu nje?” kubuza 
uThobile emva kokuba sekuvunyelenwe ngokuthi kubonanwe 
nabakwaLanga. 

“Ngokwenqubo yesiZulu, yena usenalo ilungelo lokuguqukela 
esibongweni sikayise njengoba uyise esehlawulile wakhipha 
nengezamuzi. Izingane zabafana lezi zithanda kabi ukuguqukela 
ezibongweni zoyise. Kazikunaki ukuthi oyise labo bangabantu 
abanjani, nokuthi bazikhiphile yini izimfanelo,” kuphawula 
uMaNdelu elungisa isitishi sejezi abe elinitha. 

“Ungalokothi wenze leyo nto wena Nqoba. Uyolahlekelwa 
ngamakilayenti akho. Ukhumbule ukuthi amakilayenti akho azi 
u-Advocate Mzobe, awamazi u-Advocate Langa. Ungalokothi 

168 



uziqhwebele imibuzo ezokuphoxa. Uyophendula uthini uma 
abantu sebelokhu bekubuza ukuthi usishintsheleni isibongo 
sakho?” kubuza uThobile ekhombisa ukungezwani nhlobo 
nokuthi uNqoba aguqule isibongo sakhe. 

“Kanti njalo kuyingozi ukuvele uguqule isibongo sakho 
kungonakele lutho. Siguqule ngoba kukhala abadala, futhi besho 
ukuthi bakhaliswa yini. Akulungile ukuthi usingathwe ngabakini 
yonke le minyaka, uyasuka wena uyabahlamuka uyozisondeza 
kubantu abangenandaba nawe. Angikholwa wukuthi bayakwazi 
abakwaLanga njengoba ungakaze wethulwe kubona.” 

“Ayi bo Khulu; kangizosishintsha isibongo, khululekani.” 

“Kungcono-ke uma kunjalo. Ungayilungisi into engonakele 
ngoba uyobe usuyayona. Ayi, anginishiye. Sengiyozilalela mina.” 
Yasho isukuma intombi endala ithatha inaliti, insonto kanye 
naloko eyabe isikunithile. 

Akachithanga sikhathi uMaSishi; wathi angezwa ukuthi 
bavumile abakwaMzobe, balunquma nosuku, wazisa uMaZikhali 
noCynthia. Lwafika usuku, banikela khona kwaMzobe. 
Kwahanjwa ngemoto kaMaSishi, yashayelwa nguCynthia. Wabe 
esengcono kakhulu uNtuthuko, esezihambela ngaphandle

kuzwakala nasezwini ukuthi wabe eza nodatshana olwabe

“Kanti-ke akusilo neze udaba olude mzukulu. Wukuthi nje 
kayingiphethe neze kahle indaba yokungaxhumani kukaNtuthuko 
nawe. Kakwanele ukuthi sekwaxolelwana; kufanele kube khona 
ukuxhumana ngandlela thize.” Athi ukuthula uMaSishi. 

“Phela kufanele kube nguye othatha isinyathelo, njengomuntu 
omdala. Kodwa-ke angisheshe ngisho ukuthi ukusondelana 
kwami naye kungase kuhumusheke kabi kwabanye. Abanye 
abantu bangacabanga ukuthi sengizama ukuzisondeza emafeni 
akwaLanga. Angithi uyayibona into enjalo khulu?” 

“Asingaphiki nabantu mzukulu. Asenze lokho okufanele. 
Yena uyafisa ukuthi nixhumane, kodwa uyakwesaba. Uthi wena 
unezagila zemibuzo. Kunjani sihlangane erestorenti sobathathu 
ngoLwesithathu kusihlwa?” 

“Ake ngibheke idayari yami Khulu.” Kuthuleke isikhashana 
esaphenya amakhasi. “Cha, akukho lutho ngoLwesithathu 
kusihlwa. Sengiyokuzwa ngawe-ke khulu ukuthi sihlanganela 
kuphi, ngasikhathi sini. Umtshele akhululeke; sesadlula isikhathi 
semibuzo,” kuphetha uNqoba ehleka kancane, ekhumbula 
lowaya mbuzo wakhe awujikijela maqede zehla mi izinyembezi 
kuNtuthuko. 

“Ayi-ke, angikuthinte ngoLwesithathu emini sengibekise 
nendawo erestorenti. Usale kahle Mzukulu.” 

“Bye Khulu.” UNqoba wayemane ehlonipha uMaSishi nje. 
Eqinisweni wabe engafuni ukwejwayelana kakhulu noNtuthuko 
ngoba lokho kwakungase kumphathe kabi uThobile. 

UMaSishi wabuye walushaya futhi ucingo esehlele konke 

182 



mayelana nokubonana kwabo. Kwahlanganelwa erestorenti 
yaseMusgrave ngoLwesithathu kusihlwa. UNqoba benoMaSishi 
babezikhululekele nje. UNtuthuko kwamthatha isikhathi ukuba 
ancibilike, nakhona esizwa yikho ukukhululeka kwalaba abanye.

“Ungangitsheli ukuthi usufuna ukuthenga imoto kanokusho. 
Yinto yokugcina leyo. Kufanele uqale ngomuzi. Umuzi ubaluleke 
kakhulu kunemoto. Kayinasiqiniseko imoto, ungaba nayo 
namhlanje kusasa inyamalale. Bavutha bhe abafana bamaoda 
kulezi zinsuku; kanti baningi nabashayela ngezincwadi 
zokuthengwa. Bheka nje ukuthi ashayiswa kanjani amarobhothi 
kulezi zinsuku,” kukhononda uThobile ecabanga ukuthi yabe 
inhlanhlatha indodana yakhe. 

“Ngicabanga ukuthi amarobhothi ashayiswa yilabo abasuke 
bethe ukweqisa ezincathazweni. Ngikholwa wukuthi nawe Ma 
uzoyithokozela le nto engizokukhombisa yona kusasa. Wena Ma 
ubuye ukhohlwe ukuthi wazala indoda ehlakaniphile. Awubheke

ungalindeli thina sikuncome?” kubuza uThobile ehleka.

ngehora lesishiyagalombili kusasa ekuseni?” 

“Ayi, silungile leso sikhathi,” kuvuma uThobile esahleka. 
Nebala bababela khona ngakusasa ekuseni.

ukuzibamba uThobile.

wesiqumama sangempela lowaya. Awume kancane Nqoba,”

UNqoba wabona ukuthi kwabe kungakagxili emqondweni

ukuwubona lo muzi.

“Mm! Yaze yayinhle!” kubabaza uThobile ecweba izinyembezi

elokuphumula, elokudlela kanye nekhishi. Kwabe kukhona 
nekamelo elincane elinomshini wokuwasha kanye nendawo yokuayinela. 
Igaraji ngalinye labe likwazi ukuthatha izimoto ezimbili 
zime zilandelane. Womabili amagaraji abe enomnyango ongenela 
ekamelweni lokuphumula. Kulona futhi ikamelo lokuphumula

amane okulala kanye nehhovisi. Uvulande wabe umude 
ubheke olwandle, ukwazi ukubona neBeachfront uma ukuwo. 
Kwakuyohlalwa kuwo ngezinsuku zokushisa kwehlobo, kudliwe 
okwakusihlwa kubukwa imikhumbi iphuma ingena eThekwini. 
Pho mihle yini uma isikhanyise yaqhakaza, ebusuku! Kanti

ugesi! Kodwa-ke yibone lapho isihlotshiselwe izikhathi

UNqoba benoPhilile bakugwema ukuba nendumezulu 
yomshado. Umshado wabo waba mncane wadla ngokuqhakaza 
nokuba nezintwana ezinhle ezabe zingajwayelekile. 
Babezimisele ngokumema ikhulu labantu, kodwa balungiselela 
abangaphezudlwana njengoba abantu bakithi benomkhutshana 
wokuthi bathi bangamenywa nabo baphinde bameme abangane 
babo. Bashadela etendeni elabe lihlotshiswe laqhakaziswa kahle, 
lamiswa eJapanese Gardens. NguPhilile owabe eqhamuke 
nalowo mqondo, engazi ukuthi kwabe kukuyo kanye le ndawo 
lapho uNqoba benoBoysie babeke bahlanganela khona baqaqa 
inkinga kaLanga. Emva kwenkonzo yomshado nezinkulumo 
zokufisela nokuhalalisela abashadayo, kwalandela izibiliboco 
khona etendeni. Umshado waphelela eMatata sekwabiwa, 
kudliwa eyezithebe, kugcinwa namasiko. Wabe ekhona uMaSishi 
noMaZikhali kanye noCynthia kulo mshado. UNtuthuko 
wagajwa ngamahloni wagcina ngokuthumela isipho somshado. 
Imoto kaMaSishi yabe ishayelwa nguye u-Cynthia. U-Lynne waba 
ngesinye sezikhulumi eziqavile etendeni. Naye wadlulela eMatata, 
wayithanda kakhulu indawo yakhona. Wanquma ukuphinda 
avakashe ukuze ayibone kahle iNanda Dam ephezu kwewa, 
eyibuka ngezipopolo ezithatha into ekude ziyisondeze eduze. 

UMaSishi wagcina ephumelele odabeni lwamafa kaLanga. 
Wabe emelwe ngu-Lynne ngoba icala laphelela enkantolo 
yemantshi. Indlu nokunye okuningi kwabuyela ngakuyena emva 
kokuba sesitholakele isiqiniseko sokuthi umshado wakhe noLanga 
wabe uhlanganise amafa. Kazisetshenziswanga izimoto zikaLanga. 
Zabe ziyothengiswa emva komsebenzi wakhe noMaCele. 

Zaphela golokoqo izinyanga ezintathu u-Cynthia elokhu 
ebhala ecisha. Wayesabhekisisa, ecubungulisisa isimo sezinto, 

195 



engafuni ukufana nowesifazane owake wathi etheza ehlathini 
wazitholela esihle isikhafu lesi. Wacabanga ukuthi sabe siwe 
komunye wesifazane owabe edlule kulelo hlathi. Indaba yonakala 
lapho esesicosha isikhafu sikanokusho. Hawu, kanti ngufeleba 
webululu! Nhlanhla leyo ukuthi ibululu liqale lifuthe kathathu, 
lisaqaqa amazinyo, kande ligadle. 

“Phutha lini lelo MaZikhali?” kubuza uMaSishi ehlahle 
amehlo, ethukile. 

“Kufanele kucelwe kuMaCele ukuba amemukele 
uKaMadlabane.” 

“Pho kuzomiswa kanjani njengoba izingane sezize 
zayihlanganisa inkulumo?” Wabuza esathukile uMaSishi. 
Wawubona ngamehlo engqondo umsebenzi wakhe uphelela 
obala kuhle kwesithukuthuku senja sona esiphelela oboyeni. 
Washeshe wakhumbula ukuthi uMaZikhali wabe esebenzise 
‘ucishe’. “Sekufanele senze njani MaZikhali?” Wabuza emagange 
uMaSishi. “Sizothi qu kumuntu obonayo. Akusibo neze 
ubuhlakani ukwenza izinto ngokucabangela. Ngokwejwayelekile 
kuye kube wukuxolisa nokucela. Kodwa-ke siyokuzwa phambili,” 
kuphetha uMaZikhali. Bafika libaphathele izindaba ezinhle lelo 
phambili. Wabe esemukelekile uKaMadlabane. 

Kwakusaphele amasonto ambalwa udlulile umshado kaNqoba 
noPhilile ngesikhathi abakwaMzobe bethuthela eMhlanga Ridge, 
emzini wabo omusha. Kuningana okwabe kusalungiswa egcekeni 
njengokubiya nokutshala utshani, izihlahlana nezimbali. Wabe 
uqhakazile, umuhle umuzi lo. UThobile wawubuka maqede 
wahlengezela izinyembezi, ekhumbula ukuthi wayesikaze kaningi 
ukukhipha isisu, kanti uzozala lo Nqoba osegile izimanga ezinje. 
Wabona ukuthi abantu abasuke bezalwe ngendlela ethe phecelezi 
bavamisile ukugila izimanga ezinje. Wacabanga ngenkosi uDavide 

196 



waseBhayibhelini, owafisa umfazi ka-Uri maqede wenza itulo 
lokuthi u-Uri afe empini. Wathi angafa u-Uri, uDavide wangena 
umkakhe. Bazala inkosi uSolomoni owaduma ngobuhlakani 
obungandile. Kwamcacela uThobile ukuthi wonke umuntu 
uyisidalwa sikaNkulunkulu, nokuthi kayisho lutho indlela asuke 
eze ngayo emhlabeni. Noma umuntu angabukeka edelelekile 
emehlweni omphakathi, kodwa ubalulekile emehlweni oMdali 
wakhe. UThobile yamfikela ephuma engena emakamelweni 
omuzi omusha le micabango. 

“Ngena Khulu ubone ngaphakathi,” kucela uNqoba ebamba 
ukhulu wakhe ngesandla. 

“Hlebela mina Nqoba; yimali yeGAZI LEZIBI le?” Wahleka 
kancane uNqoba ngaphambi kokuthi aphendule. 

“Nayo ilekelelile khulu. Asingene ngaphakathi.” Washo 
ekhipha iduku elimhlophe ephaketheni esula lezo zinyembezana 
zenjabulo nomunyu ezabe zihlupha intombi endala. 

“Mntanomntanami, asisophinde sibizwe ngezibi. Asingene.”
